# ActorsLite strict unified-engine tracker

Primary source of truth:
- `docs/plans/ACTORSLITE_STRICT_UNIFIED_ENGINE_PLAN.md`

Supporting or superseded context only:
- `docs/plans/actors_lite.md`
- `docs/plans/factory_fabric.md`

## Tracker status

This checklist mirrors the execution order from the strict unified-engine plan.
Do not advance implementation claims past the earliest red phase.

- [x] Phase 0: Freeze direction and remove temptation
  - [x] Strict unified-engine plan is committed in repo.
  - [x] Older milestone-only ActorsLite and forward-engine Fabric docs are marked superseded for implementation.
  - [x] Prompter/supervisor guidance points to the strict unified-engine plan.
  - [x] Crate-level docs now point to the strict unified-engine plan.
  - [ ] Repo no longer relies on temporary acceptance shortcuts in active workflow.
  - [ ] Repo no longer treats phase-4 static green as the reason ActorsLite is public.

- [x] Phase 1: Build the generic lowering spine
  - [x] Create one generic semantic lowering entry point.
  - [x] Create one generic view lowering entry point.
  - [x] Stop routing shipped examples through example-specific lowering as the production path.
  - [x] Carry persistence metadata through generic lowering.
  - [x] Audit and remove business-specific lowering items, and add guardrails against introducing new ones.
  - [x] Unsupported constructs fail with explicit generic diagnostics.

- [ ] Phase 2: Replace pure hot-path execution with slot/region runtime
  - [ ] Replace mailbox-heavy pure-node execution with slot/region runtime pieces.
  - [ ] Add dirty-closure scheduling and stale-event coverage.
  - [ ] Prove deterministic quiescence behavior under tests.

- [ ] Phase 3: Implement real persistence core
  - [ ] Add real persistence adapter and browser localStorage path.
  - [ ] Remove ActorsLite persistence-disabled UI and tooling behavior.
  - [ ] Make rerun persistence survive for durable state.

- [ ] Phase 4: Finish the host bridge and retained diff path
  - [ ] Use generic HostViewIR lowering.
  - [ ] Retain stable view identity.
  - [ ] Diff and flush after quiescence only.

- [ ] Phase 5: Counter end-to-end, with persistence
  - [ ] `counter.expected` green with persistence enabled.
  - [ ] Burst-click trace green.
  - [ ] Metrics budget green.

- [ ] Phase 6: TodoMVC end-to-end, with persistence
  - [ ] `todo_mvc.expected` green with persistence enabled.
  - [ ] Edit-save trace green and not skipped.
  - [ ] Unaffected item scopes/focus survive sibling changes.

- [ ] Phase 7: Cells and cells_dynamic, with persistence and speed
  - [ ] `cells.expected` green with persistence enabled.
  - [ ] `cells_dynamic.expected` green with persistence enabled.
  - [ ] No browser freeze on repeated edit flows.
  - [ ] No full-grid recompute on steady-state edit.
  - [ ] Performance budgets green without spreadsheet-specific code.

- [ ] Phase 8: Remove temporary mechanisms and cut over to the one engine
  - [ ] Retire example-specific lowering as the production path.
  - [ ] Remove static-green acceptance gating.
  - [ ] Remove ActorsLite `skip_persistence` verification usage.
  - [ ] Remove runtime fallbacks and persistence-disabled UI branches.
  - [ ] Stop presenting Fabric as a competing future-main-engine direction.

- [ ] Phase 9: Broader catalog parity and cleanup
  - [ ] Exposed ActorsLite examples really run.
  - [ ] Unsupported examples are hidden rather than falsely exposed.
  - [ ] Docs and developer workflows reflect one forward engine.

## Current blockers

- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/dispatch.rs` no longer has a production fallback-only classifier, `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lib.rs` no longer special-cases `Cells`, and `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lowered_preview.rs` now routes `cells` / `cells_dynamic` through the same shared lowered preview entry used by the rest of the supported/public ActorsLite catalog. `todo_mvc_physical` remains retired from the supported/public ActorsLite catalog because it is a historical multi-file physical-scene demo rather than a strict-plan proof target.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now provides a real generic HostViewIR path for `cells` / `cells_dynamic`: `LoweredProgram::into_host_view()` returns the generic retained host tree, `lower_view(...)` succeeds for both sheets, and the retained host path now covers the shared cells row/cell identities and editing input nodes. `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/cells_preview.rs` still exists for tests and metrics, but its runtime surface now sits on the generic `HostViewPreviewApp` shell instead of the old runtime-backed tree.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now routes `complex_counter`, `list_map_external_dep`, `list_map_block`, `list_retain_count`, `list_object_state`, `list_retain_remove`, `shopping_list`, `chained_list_remove_bug`, `crud`, `layers`, `pages`, `text_interpolation_update`, `button_hover_to_click_test`, `button_hover_test`, `filter_checkbox_bug`, `checkbox_test`, `while_function_call`, `switch_hold_test`, `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, `timer`, `circle_drawer`, and `cells` through parser-backed structural matching from `parse_static_expressions(...)` instead of relying on raw source-marker checks in the production path. `lower_program(...)` now runs as one ordered lowering pipeline over a shared parsed lowering context, that pipeline now groups counter, interval, display, local-state, form-runtime, list, timed-flow, and terminal host-view surfaces behind shared family dispatcher steps instead of keeping each one as its own top-level entry, and the timed-flow, local-state, form-runtime, list-family, and parts of the counter/terminal host-view families now share generic parse-layer binding/function/alias/call-path/text validation helpers instead of open-coding those checks per surface. The `list_retain_count` / `list_retain_remove` / `shopping_list` append-on-enter family now also shares one lowerer-owned append-list validation/helper path and one shared IR builder instead of duplicating that input/list/count runtime per surface, while `list_retain_count` / `list_retain_remove` also share one plain append-list HostView document helper instead of duplicating that retained tree layout per surface; `list_map_external_dep` / `list_map_block` / `list_retain_count` / `list_retain_remove` now also share one retained mapped-label node builder and one mapped-label stripe HostView helper instead of each hand-rolling the same mapped label list wrappers, while `shopping_list` now shares that same repeated mapped-label helper through a styled-label mode instead of hand-building its mapped grocery rows; `list_object_state` now shares one mapped button-label row HostView helper instead of hand-building each retained button-plus-label row; `shopping_list` and `circle_drawer` now also share one button-plus-label action-row HostView helper instead of each hand-building the same small retained row shell around a status label and action button, while `filter_checkbox_bug` / `checkbox_test` / `chained_list_remove_bug` now also share one checkbox-list document helper on top of their already shared plain-button-row and mapped-checkbox-row helpers instead of each hand-building a slightly different document/container shell; `shopping_list`, `temperature_converter`, `timer`, `circle_drawer`, and `crud` now also share one titled-column HostView document shell instead of each hand-building the same document-plus-column-plus-title wrapper, while `list_retain_reactive`, `list_map_external_dep`, `list_map_block`, `list_retain_count`, `list_retain_remove`, and `list_object_state` now also share one flat-stripe HostView document family instead of splitting the same document-then-stripe shell across separate filterable-list, append-list, mapped-list, and object-state wrappers; `text_interpolation_update` and `while_function_call` now share one lowerer-owned conditional-label capability for bool-driven `WHEN` / `WHILE` text branches instead of bespoke document helpers, while `switch_hold_test` now also uses the shared generic `WHEN` / `WHILE` subtree lowering path instead of a bespoke document shell; `pages` and the CRUD action row still share one configurable styled-button-row HostView helper instead of duplicating the retained button-strip layout per surface; the `temperature_converter` / `flight_booker` / `timer` form-runtime family now shares one structural validation helper instead of duplicating hold-heavy document/alias/function/text checks per surface; `todo_mvc`, `todo_mvc_physical`, `layers`, `pages`, `latest`, `list_map_external_dep`, `list_map_block`, `list_retain_reactive`, `text_interpolation_update`, the timed `then` / `when` / `while` family, and `chained_list_remove_bug` / `crud` now also use the shared structural validator instead of open-coding their top-level binding/function/call-path/text gates; the timed `then` / `when` / `while` family now also shares one lowerer-owned `sum_of_steps` extraction and timer-backed HostView builder plus the shared hold-backed timed-input IR scaffolding used by `then` / `when`, instead of duplicating that setup per surface; `complex_counter`, `list_object_state`, `while_function_call`, `button_hover_to_click_test`, `button_hover_test`, `switch_hold_test`, and `circle_drawer` already use that same shared structural validator for their binding/function/alias/call-path/text gates; `fibonacci` now also uses the generic retained HostView path by lowering `message |> Document/new()` through `lower_generic_host_view(...)`, `layers` now also uses the generic retained HostView path by lowering `Document/new(root: Element/stack(...))` through `lower_generic_host_view(...)`, `complex_counter` now also uses the generic retained HostView path by lowering its `PASS`/`PASSED`-driven button stripe through `lower_generic_host_view(...)` instead of a bespoke document builder, `interval` / `interval_hold` now also use the generic retained HostView path plus the shared timer-source appender instead of a bespoke interval document helper, `button_hover_to_click_test` now also uses the generic retained HostView path instead of a bespoke simple-column document helper, `button_hover_test` now also uses the generic retained HostView path instead of a bespoke styled-button-row document helper, `temperature_converter` now also uses the generic retained HostView path instead of a bespoke titled-form document helper, `flight_booker` now also uses the generic retained HostView path instead of a bespoke titled-form document helper, `timer` now also uses the generic retained HostView path plus the shared timer-source appender instead of a bespoke timer document helper, and `circle_drawer` now also uses the generic retained HostView path instead of a bespoke canvas document helper; the generic view lowerer now accepts the piped `Document/new()` wrapper directly, supports `Element/stack(...)` plus styled positioned `Element/container(...)` nodes, supports `Element/svg(...)` plus mapped `Element/svg_circle(...)` children through the retained `AbsoluteCanvas` / `PositionedCircleList` host path, supports `Element/text_input(...)`, `Element/slider(...)`, and now `Element/select(...)` through generic retained control lowering, supports LINK-origin fallback sinks for linked control `selected` / `disabled` state when the source view keeps static literals at the control site, supports `BLOCK { ... }` scoped bindings and `|> LINK { ... }` setters directly at view sites, assigns deterministic synthetic origin identities and fallback press ports to direct user-function view calls that return buttons, resolves `PASS`/`PASSED` aliases in generic view environments including inherited/nested `PASS` object fields, resolves static nested binding paths that pass through function-produced object values, supports local sink-bound view aliases for retained controls, supports multi-sink templated text labels, now also supports templated/sink-backed button labels plus bool-driven `WHEN` / `WHILE` conditional-label lowering, resolves top-level text-producing function calls during generic text lowering, supports root-bound sink fallback when a top-level `Document/new()` wraps a non-view signal pipeline, supports bool-driven `WHEN` / `WHILE` button background and outline styles, supports `Fill` control widths in the generic styled-control path, and now lowers the hover-reactive rounded `Element/button(...)` shapes used by `complex_counter`, `button_hover_to_click_test`, and `button_hover_test` through generic styled-button extraction instead of requiring bespoke HostView builders; and the old dead per-surface HostView builders for `counter`, `complex_counter`, `latest`, `layers`, `interval`, `flight_booker`, `button_hover_to_click_test`, `button_hover_test`, `text_interpolation_update`, `while_function_call`, `temperature_converter`, `timer`, `circle_drawer`, the legacy `then` / `when` / `while` arithmetic views, and the old single-label `fibonacci` document helper have now been removed from the production lowerer instead of lingering beside the generic path. Phase 1 is still red because that pipeline still dispatches into many per-surface lowerers rather than a unified semantic/view lowering mechanism.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also moves `pages` onto the generic retained HostView path: the route-matched content subtree lowers through the shared `MatchGroup` host path via a shared `current_page` sink, and the navigation buttons now use a shared LINK-origin active-style fallback instead of the bespoke `lower_pages_document()` builder.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` no longer keeps thin production document-forwarding wrappers for `list_retain_reactive`, `list_map_external_dep`, `list_map_block`, `list_retain_count`, `list_retain_remove`, `list_object_state`, `shopping_list`, `filter_checkbox_bug`, `checkbox_test`, `chained_list_remove_bug`, or `crud`. Those production call sites now invoke the shared flat-stripe, checkbox-list, titled-column, and styled-button-row document families directly, which removes another layer of per-surface HostView lowering without changing runtime behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the structural-validation-plus-flat-stripe-document shape for `list_retain_reactive`, `list_map_external_dep`, `list_map_block`, and `list_object_state` through one shared `lower_validated_flat_stripe_document(...)` helper instead of having each surface separately run `top_level_bindings(...)` plus `require_structural_validation(...)` plus `lower_flat_stripe_document(...)`. This still leaves per-surface semantic entry points and sink/runtime choices in place, but it removes another repeated production lowering slice from the list family.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` also no longer keeps a separate `lower_todo_document(...)` production wrapper around `IrExecutor` plus template materialization. `try_lower_todo_mvc_from_expressions(...)` now materializes the `todo_mvc` host tree directly from the lowered IR via the shared `todo_host_view_sink_values(...)` plus `materialize_host_view_template(...)` path, leaving the remaining specialization explicit in the template data rather than hidden behind another per-surface lowering step.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also pushes the append-list trio one step further into a shared semantic family helper: `list_retain_count`, `list_retain_remove`, and `shopping_list` all enter through one lowerer-owned `lower_append_list_family_runtime(...)` path that runs family validation and base append-list runtime construction together before each surface adds only its specific sinks or HostView shell. The old per-surface append-list IR builder functions are gone, so this family now shares more than just isolated runtime/document helpers.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the append-list flat-stripe HostView shell for `list_retain_count` and `list_retain_remove` through one shared `lower_append_list_flat_stripe_document(...)` helper instead of having each surface separately assemble the same input-plus-count-plus-mapped-list retained tree with only minor title/count-label differences. `shopping_list` still uses its own titled-column shell, but another repeated append-list production HostView slice is now centralized.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also trims the ordered lowering spine itself: `list_retain_reactive` is folded into the main list family step, and `while_function_call` / `switch_hold_test` are folded into the same local-state family step as the other toggle examples instead of keeping separate top-level pipeline entries. This does not finish Phase 1, but it does remove more per-surface dispatch structure from `LOWERING_PIPELINE`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also folds `todo_mvc` into the main list family step instead of keeping it as its own top-level pipeline entry. This is still not the end-state unified semantic lowering the plan requires, but it removes another singleton branch from `LOWERING_PIPELINE` while leaving the current runtime/host behavior unchanged.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the shared bool-toggle HOLD spine for `list_retain_reactive` and `list_map_external_dep` through one lowerer-owned `lower_bool_toggle_runtime(...)` helper instead of having each surface hand-roll the same source/not/then/hold/mode-label runtime nodes. This is still a family helper, not the final unified semantic lowering, but it removes another repeated per-surface runtime slice from the list family.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the already-generic `pages`, `latest`, `text_interpolation_update`, `while_function_call`, `button_hover_to_click_test`, `button_hover_test`, and `switch_hold_test` surfaces through one shared `lower_validated_generic_host_view(...)` helper instead of open-coding the same `top_level_bindings(...)` plus `require_structural_validation(...)` plus `lower_generic_host_view(...)` sequence in each per-surface lowerer. This still leaves per-surface semantic entry points in place, but it removes another repeated lowering shape from the display/local-state families.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes `complex_counter` and `circle_drawer` through that same shared `lower_validated_generic_host_view(...)` helper instead of open-coding structural validation immediately followed by generic retained HostView lowering in those per-surface lowerers. Their IR construction still remains surface-specific, but another repeated validation-plus-host-view production slice is now centralized.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the simple `counter` surface through that same shared `lower_validated_generic_host_view(...)` helper instead of dropping directly from bespoke counter binding extraction into `lower_generic_host_view(...)`. The numeric-runtime extraction for `counter` still remains custom, but the retained HostView side now follows the same shared validation-plus-host-view path as the rest of the counter/display family.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes TodoMVC template materialization through one shared `materialize_todo_host_view_from_sink_values(...)` helper instead of open-coding the same sink-value expansion plus `materialize_host_view_template(&todo_host_view_template(), ...)` sequence in both the `TodoProgram` materializer and the production `try_lower_todo_mvc_from_expressions(...)` path. This does not yet make todo semantic lowering generic, but it removes another repeated production HostView step from the remaining non-generic path.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the checkbox-list family surfaces `filter_checkbox_bug`, `checkbox_test`, and `chained_list_remove_bug` through one shared `lower_validated_checkbox_list_document(...)` helper instead of open-coding the same structural-validation-plus-checkbox-document sequence in each per-surface lowerer. This still leaves per-surface semantic entry points and sink/port assignments in place, but it removes another repeated list-family lowering shape from the production path.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the already-generic `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, `timer`, and `layers` surfaces through the shared `lower_validated_generic_host_view(...)` helper instead of open-coding the same validation-plus-generic-host-view sequence in each per-surface lowerer. `timer` still appends its timer source afterward, and each surface still owns its specific IR and sink/port wiring, but another repeated form/display lowering shape is now centralized.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the timed `then` / `when` / `while` family through one shared `lower_timed_flow_program_base(...)` helper instead of having each surface separately reassemble the same timed-input sinks, button ports, shared generic HostView wiring, and result sink plumbing around the already-shared timed-flow base. This still leaves the family-specific IR builders in place, but it removes another repeated program-assembly shape from the timed-flow family.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the `interval` / `interval_hold` timer-backed signal family through one shared `lower_timer_backed_signal_program(...)` helper instead of having each surface separately reassemble the same `IntervalProgram` shell around the already-shared timer-backed retained HostView path. This still leaves the family-specific signal validation and IR builders in place, but it removes another repeated program-assembly shape from the timer-backed signal family.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the hold-backed `counter_hold` and `complex_counter` accumulator runtime through one shared `lower_counter_accumulator_runtime(...)` helper instead of having those surfaces separately hand-build the same press-port-plus-delta-to-held-counter node chain. This still leaves the simple `counter` stream form and the per-surface validation/host wiring in place, but it removes another repeated semantic/runtime slice from the counter family.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the `fibonacci`, `layers`, and static-document sink-value display paths through shared `lower_generic_host_view_with_sink_values(...)` / `lower_validated_generic_host_view_with_sink_values(...)` helpers instead of having each surface separately pair generic retained HostView lowering with a one-off fixed sink-value map assembly. This still leaves surface-specific validation and value derivation in place, but it removes another repeated display-program assembly shape from the production lowerer.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the remaining titled-column production HostView family through a shared `TitledColumnDocumentConfig` path: `shopping_list` and `crud` both now build their titled retained column shell through `lower_titled_column_document_from_config(...)`, while `crud` also routes its structural-validation-plus-titled-column step through `lower_validated_titled_column_document(...)` instead of open-coding validation and then calling the raw positional titled-column builder directly. Their semantic/runtime lowering still remains surface-specific, but another repeated production HostView slice is now centralized.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the repeated `top_level_bindings(...)` plus `require_structural_validation(...)` sequence behind one shared `validated_top_level_bindings(...)` helper. The remaining direct Todo paths (`todo_mvc`, `todo_mvc_physical`) plus the shared validated generic-host-view, checkbox-list, flat-stripe, titled-column, and timed-flow family helpers now all use that one parser-backed validation entry instead of repeating the same binding-and-validation scaffold at each call site.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining “reuse the already-built binding map while lowering the generic retained host view” path behind one shared `lower_generic_host_view_from_bindings(...)` helper. The simple `counter` lowerer and the shared timed-flow family base now both reuse their existing binding/validation work when lowering the generic HostView shell instead of recomputing that path through a second generic-host-view entry.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the append-list family’s remaining parser-backed binding extraction behind one shared `validated_append_list_bindings(...)` entry. `list_retain_count`, `list_retain_remove`, and `shopping_list` no longer open-code `top_level_bindings(...)` before entering the shared append-list validation/runtime helper; that family helper now owns both binding extraction and append-list validation before building the shared runtime shell.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the “semantic IR already needed bindings, but the shared flat-stripe host helper revalidated by rebuilding them” path behind `lower_validated_flat_stripe_document_from_bindings(...)`. `list_retain_reactive` now reuses its existing parser-backed binding map for both semantic IR extraction and structural validation before lowering the shared flat-stripe retained shell instead of making the shared host helper rebuild those bindings a second time.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the matching generic-host-view path behind `lower_validated_generic_host_view_from_bindings(...)`. The simple `counter` lowerer and the shared timed-flow family base now reuse their already-built binding maps for structural validation plus generic retained HostView lowering instead of open-coding that validation-plus-host step, and the older raw-expression sink-value helper is now gone because all remaining sink-value sites already route through the binding-aware path.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the pure retained generic-host surfaces behind one shared `GenericHostSurfaceConfig` path. `pages`, `latest`, `text_interpolation_update`, `while_function_call`, `button_hover_test`, and `switch_hold_test` now all route their host-only structural spec plus sink/source/view wiring through `lower_generic_host_surface(...)` instead of each open-coding the same validated generic-host invocation shape, while their surface-specific sink/port exposure still remains local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the retained sink-value display surfaces behind shared `GenericHostSinkValuesSurfaceConfig` / `GenericHostSinkValuesFromBindingsConfig` helpers. `layers` now routes its validated retained host-plus-fixed-sink-values path through the new config-owned helper, while `fibonacci` and `static_document` route their already-binding-aware host-plus-sink-values paths through the matching binding-owned helper instead of each open-coding that generic retained display assembly shape.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining direct flat-stripe retained-view surfaces behind one shared `FlatStripeSurfaceConfig` path. `list_map_external_dep`, `list_map_block`, and `list_object_state` now all route their structural spec plus flat-stripe document shell through `lower_flat_stripe_surface(...)` instead of each open-coding the same validated flat-stripe invocation shape, while their semantic/runtime outputs and public sink/port exposure still remain local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the checkbox-list retained-view family behind one shared `CheckboxListSurfaceConfig` path. `filter_checkbox_bug`, `checkbox_test`, and `chained_list_remove_bug` now all route their structural spec plus checkbox-list document shell through `lower_checkbox_list_surface(...)` instead of each open-coding the same validated checkbox-list invocation shape, while their semantic/runtime outputs and public sink/port exposure still remain local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining direct “semantic/runtime IR plus generic retained HostView shell” path behind one shared `GenericHostIrSurfaceConfig` helper. `complex_counter`, `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, `timer`, `button_hover_to_click_test`, and `circle_drawer` now all route their validated generic retained host-view shell through `lower_generic_host_ir_surface(...)`, while `timer` also carries its appended timer source through the same shared config instead of hand-appending that child after a one-off validated generic-host call.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the append-list family’s remaining final retained HostView shell behind one shared `AppendListHostViewConfig` entry. `list_retain_count`, `list_retain_remove`, and `shopping_list` now all route their already-shared append-list runtime output through `lower_append_list_host_view(...)` instead of each directly picking between `lower_append_list_flat_stripe_document(...)` and `lower_titled_column_document_from_config(...)` at the production call site.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining binding-aware “semantic/runtime IR plus generic retained HostView shell” path behind `lower_generic_host_ir_from_bindings(...)`. The simple `counter` lowerer and the timed `then` / `when` / `while` family base now both reuse their already-built binding maps while routing timer-source children through the same shared IR-host helper instead of open-coding `lower_validated_generic_host_view_from_bindings(...)` plus manual timer-child appends.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the template-backed semantic/runtime lowering flow behind `lower_template_backed_ir_surface(...)`. `todo_mvc` now routes its validated bindings, persistence-aware IR construction, executor pass, and HostViewTemplate materialization through that shared helper instead of open-coding the validate/build/execute/materialize sequence at the production call site.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the simple counter runtime behind the shared `lower_counter_accumulator_runtime(...)` helper. The non-`HOLD` `counter` path still validates the source-level `LATEST { ... } |> Math/sum()` shape, but it now lowers through the same shared seed-plus-delta accumulator runtime as `counter_hold` / `complex_counter` instead of keeping a bespoke `Latest`/`MathSum` node chain at the production call site.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the timed-flow family’s accumulating timer inputs behind `append_accumulating_timed_input(...)`. `then` / `when` now layer persistence on top of that shared helper through the existing hold-backed wrapper, and `while` now reuses the same accumulator runtime without introducing persistence metadata instead of keeping a separate `MathSum`/`Latest` timer-input chain at the production call site.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the filtered-list toggle runtime behind one shared `lower_toggle_selected_list_ir(...)` helper. `list_retain_reactive` now routes its persisted even-filter toggle, selected-list choice, and derived count label through that shared helper, and `list_map_external_dep` now uses the same helper with static text branches instead of keeping a bespoke object-list plus function-template lowering path for the same toggle-selected-list behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining validation-only and titled-column retained-surface paths behind shared `lower_validation_only_surface(...)` and `lower_titled_column_surface(...)` helpers. `todo_mvc_physical` no longer open-codes a one-off validation-only lowerer, and `crud` now routes its validation plus titled-column retained shell through the same surface helper instead of calling the raw validated document builder directly at the production site.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining host-only flat-stripe retained surfaces behind `lower_flat_stripe_host_only_surface(...)`. `list_map_block` and `list_object_state` no longer call the raw flat-stripe retained surface builder directly at their production sites; both now route their validation plus host-only flat-stripe shell through that shared entry while keeping their exposed sink/port arrays local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the hold-backed timed-math runtime behind one shared `lower_hold_backed_timed_math_ir(...)` helper. `then` and `when` no longer hand-assemble separate persisted timed-input plus event-triggered add/subtract node chains; both now reuse the same lowerer-owned helper with only their action set and base ids differing.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the accumulating timed-hold core behind `append_accumulating_timed_hold(...)`. The timed-flow family still uses the existing sink-emitting wrapper, but `interval_hold` no longer hand-assembles its own timed hold/update chain and instead reuses the same lowerer-owned accumulator core before applying its skip-first sink behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the interval-family production surface shell behind `lower_timer_backed_signal_surface(...)`. `interval` and `interval_hold` no longer each open-code the same top-level binding extraction plus `lower_timer_backed_signal_program(...)` wiring; both now route through one timer-backed surface entry and keep only their subset-specific validation / IR builder logic local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes counter-family `IrProgram` assembly behind `lower_counter_accumulator_program(...)`. `counter`, `counter_hold`, and `complex_counter` still decide their own actions and persistence semantics locally, but they no longer each hand-wrap the shared accumulator runtime into separate `IrProgram { nodes, functions: Vec::new(), persistence: ... }` shapes at the production call sites.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the append-list production surface shell behind `lower_append_list_surface(...)`. `list_retain_remove`, `shopping_list`, and the augmented `list_retain_count` path no longer each open-code the same `lower_append_list_family_runtime(...)` plus `lower_append_list_host_view(...)` pairing; they now share one lowerer-owned surface entry and keep only their subset-specific validation / IR augmentation local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining “finished `IrProgram` plus generic retained HostView shell” pairing behind `lower_generic_host_ir_program_surface(...)`. `complex_counter`, `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, `timer`, and `circle_drawer` no longer each open-code `ir: ...` immediately followed by `host_view: lower_generic_host_ir_surface(...)`; they now share one lowerer-owned surface helper and keep only their subset-specific IR construction and exported sink/port ids local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining host-only generic retained-surface wrapper behind `lower_generic_host_surface_program(...)`. `pages`, `latest`, `text_interpolation_update`, `while_function_call`, `button_hover_test`, and `switch_hold_test` no longer each open-code `host_view: lower_generic_host_surface(...)` directly at the production site; they now share one lowerer-owned host-only generic surface entry and keep only their exposed sink/port ids local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the checkbox-list program wrapper behind `lower_checkbox_list_surface_program(...)`. `filter_checkbox_bug`, `checkbox_test`, and `chained_list_remove_bug` no longer each open-code `host_view: lower_checkbox_list_surface(...)` directly at the production site; they now share one lowerer-owned checkbox-list surface-program entry and keep only their exposed sink/port ids local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the host-only flat-stripe program wrapper behind `lower_flat_stripe_host_only_surface_program(...)`. `list_map_block` and `list_object_state` no longer each open-code `host_view: lower_flat_stripe_host_only_surface(...)` directly at the production site; they now share one lowerer-owned host-only flat-stripe surface-program entry and keep only their exposed sink/port ids local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining validated flat-stripe program wrappers behind `lower_flat_stripe_surface_program(...)` and `lower_flat_stripe_surface_program_from_bindings(...)`. `list_map_external_dep` no longer open-codes `host_view: lower_flat_stripe_surface(...)`, and `list_retain_reactive` no longer open-codes the binding-aware `host_view: lower_validated_flat_stripe_document_from_bindings(...)`; both now route through shared lowerer-owned flat-stripe program entries and keep only their IR plus exposed sink/port ids local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the last direct titled-column / generic-host-IR program wrappers behind `lower_titled_column_surface_program(...)` and `lower_generic_host_ir_surface_program(...)`. `crud` no longer open-codes `let host_view = lower_titled_column_surface(...); Ok(CrudProgram { host_view, ... })`, and `button_hover_to_click_test` no longer open-codes `host_view: lower_generic_host_ir_surface(...)` directly at the production site; both now route through shared lowerer-owned surface-program entries and keep only their exposed sink/port ids local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining “parse bindings first, then materialize generic retained host view with parsed context” seam behind `lower_bindings_with_host_view(...)`. `counter` no longer open-codes `top_level_bindings(...)` immediately followed by binding-local port extraction plus `lower_generic_host_ir_from_bindings(...)`, and the timed `then` / `when` / `while` family base no longer open-codes the same bindings-first parse-plus-host-view shape for its timer inputs; both now route through one lowerer-owned bindings/materialization helper and keep only their subset-specific parsed context local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining tuple-return program wrappers behind `lower_template_backed_ir_surface_program(...)` and `lower_generic_host_surface_with_sink_values_from_bindings_program(...)`. `todo_mvc` no longer open-codes `let (ir, host_view) = lower_template_backed_ir_surface(...); Ok(TodoProgram { ir, host_view, ... })`, and the static-document path no longer open-codes `let (host_view, sink_values) = lower_generic_host_surface_with_sink_values_from_bindings(...); Ok(StaticProgram { host_view, sink_values })`; both now route through shared lowerer-owned surface-program entries and keep only their subset-specific IR or sink-value construction local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining “collect top-level bindings, then hand them to another shared lowerer” boilerplate behind `lower_with_bindings(...)`. The generic-host-IR entry, the timer-backed `interval` / `interval_hold` surface, the validated append-list / structural binding collectors, `list_retain_reactive`, and the static-document path no longer each call `top_level_bindings(...)` inline before immediately delegating to another lowerer-owned step; they now share one bindings-first helper and keep only their subset-specific post-binding work local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining generic-host-IR tuple-program wrapper behind `lower_generic_host_ir_program(...)`. `complex_counter`, `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, `timer`, and `circle_drawer` no longer each open-code `let (ir, host_view) = lower_generic_host_ir_program_surface(...); Ok(Program { ir, host_view, ... })`; they now share one lowerer-owned generic-host-IR program entry and keep only their subset-specific sink/port ids local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining append-list tuple-program wrappers and validated fixed-sink-value host-only wrapper behind `lower_append_list_surface_program(...)` and `lower_generic_host_surface_with_sink_values_program(...)`. `list_retain_count`, `list_retain_remove`, and `shopping_list` no longer each open-code `let (ir, host_view) = lower_append_list_surface(...); Ok(Program { ir, host_view, ... })`, and `layers` no longer open-codes `let (host_view, sink_values) = lower_generic_host_surface_with_sink_values(...); Ok(LayersProgram { ... })`; together with the already-shared bindings-aware sink-values program path now reused by `fibonacci`, these families now route through lowerer-owned program wrappers and keep only their subset-specific IR or exported sink/port ids local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining timed-flow typed-program wrapper behind `lower_timed_flow_program(...)`. `then`, `when`, and `while` no longer each open-code `let base = lower_timed_flow_program_base(...); Ok(Program { ir: ..., host_view: base.host_view, ... })`; they now share one lowerer-owned timed-flow program entry and keep only their subset-specific IR construction plus subtraction-port requirement local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes generic HostViewIR binding collection itself through the shared `lower_with_bindings(...)` spine. `lower_generic_host_view_with_root_binding(...)` no longer calls `top_level_bindings(...)` directly before constructing `GenericViewLoweringContext`; the generic retained-view path now shares the same bindings-first lowerer-owned entry used by the higher-level surface helpers.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the remaining direct display-family binding pass through `lower_with_bindings(...)`. `fibonacci` no longer calls `top_level_bindings(...)` directly before validating its semantic bindings and delegating into the shared bindings-aware sink-values HostView path; it now uses the same lowerer-owned bindings-first entry as the rest of the production lowering spine.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining parsed-bindings generic HostViewIR path behind `lower_bindings_with_generic_host_ir(...)`. `counter` no longer open-codes “parse local semantic context, then call `lower_generic_host_ir_from_bindings(...)`” for its increment-button binding, and the timed `then` / `when` / `while` family base no longer open-codes the same parsed-bindings-plus-generic-HostViewIR shape for its timer inputs; both now share one lowerer-owned bindings/context/HostView helper and keep only their subset-specific semantic parsing local.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the validated generic retained HostView surface path through `lower_with_bindings(...)`. `lower_validated_generic_host_view(...)` no longer calls `top_level_bindings(...)` directly before delegating to the bindings-aware validation/helper path; the validated host-only generic surface family now shares the same lowerer-owned bindings-first entry as the rest of the production spine.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also folds `circle_drawer`, `cells`, and the static-document path into the main display/terminal retained-view family step instead of keeping a separate terminal-host-view top-level pipeline branch. This still leaves those per-surface lowerers in place, but it removes another singleton top-level branch from `LOWERING_PIPELINE` while preserving the same attempt order.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/parse.rs` now preserves persistence ids, owns the shared nested-binding lookup, and exposes shared persistence-entry helpers for both bindings and binding paths; `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the live persistence-bearing lowering sites through one shared lowerer-owned `LoweringPersistenceSpec` collector with explicit hold/list-store constructors instead of having each site call the parser helpers directly. `counter_hold`, the generic `todo_mvc` list hold, `list_retain_reactive`, the timed `then`/`when` input holds, and the `cells` / `cells_dynamic` `overrides` list-store all now emit durable metadata through that shared parser-backed/lowerer-owned persistence-plan path. Phase 1 is still red because persistence derivation still originates from per-surface lowering decisions about what should persist, rather than from one unified semantic lowering mechanism.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also moves part of the production fallback pipeline off the per-example `try_lower_*` wrappers and onto direct lowerer-owned family attempts. Inside `lower_toggle_local_state_family_step(...)`, `text_interpolation_update`, `button_hover_test`, `while_function_call`, and `switch_hold_test` no longer route through separate expression-step shims as the main `lower_program(...)` path; the pipeline now lowers those host-only retained examples directly through shared `lower_generic_host_surface_program(...)` family entries while preserving the same attempt order and keeping the typed `try_lower_*` functions only as explicit typed entry points.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also moves more of the display-family production pipeline off the per-example `try_lower_*` wrappers and onto direct lowerer-owned family attempts. Inside `lower_display_family_step(...)`, `pages` and `latest` no longer route through separate expression-step shims as the main `lower_program(...)` path; the pipeline now lowers both host-only retained examples directly through shared `lower_generic_host_surface_program(...)` family entries while preserving the same attempt order and keeping the typed `try_lower_*` functions only as explicit typed entry points.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also moves the remaining pure display helper wrappers for `fibonacci` and `layers` off the production fallback pipeline and into direct lowerer-owned family attempts. Inside `lower_display_family_step(...)`, both examples now lower directly through the shared bindings-first sink-value host-view entry or the shared fixed-sink-value host-surface entry, rather than routing the main `lower_program(...)` path through separate expression-step shims; the typed `try_lower_*` functions remain only as explicit typed entry points.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also moves the interval family off the production fallback expression-step wrappers and into direct lowerer-owned family attempts. Inside `lower_interval_family_step(...)`, `interval` and `interval_hold` no longer route through separate `try_lower_*` step shims as the main `lower_program(...)` path; the pipeline now lowers both through the shared `lower_timer_backed_signal_surface(...)` family entry while preserving attempt order and keeping the typed `try_lower_*` functions only as explicit typed entry points.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining typed-expression family dispatch through one shared lowerer-owned wrapper. `lower_counter_family_step(...)`, `lower_form_runtime_family_step(...)`, `lower_list_family_step(...)`, and `lower_timed_flow_family_step(...)` no longer route the main `lower_program(...)` path through private `lower_*_step` wrappers for `counter`, `complex_counter`, `todo_mvc`, `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, `timer`, `list_map_external_dep`, `list_map_block`, `list_retain_count`, `list_object_state`, `chained_list_remove_bug`, `crud`, `list_retain_remove`, `shopping_list`, `list_retain_reactive`, `then`, `when`, and `while`; they now all use one shared `lower_typed_expression_program(...)` path while keeping the typed `try_lower_*_from_expressions(...)` entry points themselves intact.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the last display-family step-wrapper tail from the main production pipeline. Inside `lower_display_family_step(...)`, `circle_drawer`, `cells`, and the static-document path no longer route through private `lower_*_step` wrappers; the production display family now lowers all three directly through the shared `lower_typed_expression_program(...)` path while keeping the typed `try_lower_circle_drawer_from_expressions(...)`, `try_lower_cells_program_from_expressions(...)`, and `try_lower_static_document_from_expressions(...)` entry points intact.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the last toggle-family step-wrapper island and the obsolete `define_expr_lowering_step!` macro. Inside `lower_toggle_local_state_family_step(...)`, `button_hover_to_click_test`, `filter_checkbox_bug`, and `checkbox_test` no longer route through private `lower_*_step` wrappers; the toggle-local-state production family now lowers those typed-expression examples directly through the shared `lower_typed_expression_program(...)` path while keeping the typed `try_lower_*_from_expressions(...)` entry points intact.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining family-local labeled-attempt control flow through one shared lowerer-owned helper. The toggle-local-state, interval, and display families no longer each open-code their own `match ... { Ok(program) => return Matched(program), Err(error) => errors.push((label, error)) }` control flow around `lower_generic_host_surface_program(...)`, `lower_generic_host_surface_with_sink_values_program(...)`, `lower_with_bindings(...)`, or `lower_timer_backed_signal_surface(...)`; those family-local generic-host / timer-backed / sink-value attempts now all route through one shared `lower_labeled_program(...)` path while preserving the same attempt order and subset-specific lowering logic.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the single-entry persistence spec/resolution path through shared lowerer-owned helpers. The durable list-store path in `todo_mvc`, the durable hold path in the timed hold-backed inputs, and the durable hold/list-store spec sites in `counter_hold` and `list_retain_reactive` no longer each hand-assemble one-off `collect_lowering_persistence(...)` or raw `LoweringPersistenceSpec::*` vectors inline; those persistence-bearing lowerers now share `hold_binding_persistence_spec(...)`, `hold_path_persistence_spec(...)`, `list_store_path_persistence_spec(...)`, `collect_single_lowering_persistence(...)`, `collect_hold_path_persistence(...)`, and `collect_list_store_path_persistence(...)` while preserving the same durable metadata and node/slot assignments.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/parse.rs` now also exposes shared parser-backed vector helpers for single durable persistence entries, and `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/cells_preview.rs` now routes its durable overrides metadata through them. The `cells` / `cells_dynamic` lowerer no longer hand-builds its one-entry `IrProgram.persistence` vector by calling `persist_entry_for_binding(...).into_iter().collect()` directly; it now shares the parser-backed `persist_entries_for_path(...)` path, matching the lowerer-owned persistence helper direction already used for other durable hold/list-store sites while preserving the same durable list-store metadata for `CellsProgram::OVERRIDES_LIST_HOLD_NODE`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the typed family-attempt dispatch loops behind one shared lowerer-owned runner plus explicit family attempt tables. The counter, form-runtime, timed-flow, and list families no longer open-code long chains of identical `match lower_typed_expression_program(...)` branches, and the toggle/display families now also share the same runner for their typed-entry tails while preserving attempt order around the remaining direct generic-host-surface attempts. This removes another repeated per-surface production-lowering shell from the ordered lowering spine without changing the typed entry points themselves.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining host-only/timer-backed family dispatch loops behind one shared lowerer-owned contextual runner plus explicit family attempt tables. The toggle-local-state, interval, and display families no longer open-code long chains of identical `match lower_labeled_program(...)` and mixed typed/generic-host-surface attempts in the main `lower_program(...)` path; they now route those ordered attempts through shared contextual family tables while preserving the same subset order and keeping the per-surface lowerers themselves intact as explicit typed/contextual entry points.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the typed interval/display/host-only-toggle entry points back through that shared contextual family spine instead of duplicating the same lowering bodies beside it. `try_lower_interval*_from_expressions(...)`, `try_lower_fibonacci_from_expressions(...)`, `try_lower_layers_from_expressions(...)`, `try_lower_pages_from_expressions(...)`, `try_lower_latest_from_expressions(...)`, `try_lower_text_interpolation_update_from_expressions(...)`, `try_lower_while_function_call_from_expressions(...)`, `try_lower_button_hover_test_from_expressions(...)`, and `try_lower_switch_hold_test_from_expressions(...)` now delegate through one shared `lower_contextual_program(...)` bridge into the contextual family attempts, so those typed entry points no longer carry parallel per-surface lowering implementations.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the family-step outcome shell itself through shared lowerer-owned helpers. The toggle-local-state, counter, interval, display, form-runtime, timed-flow, and list family steps no longer each open-code their own `let mut errors = Vec::new(); match run_*_attempts(...) { ... }` control flow; they now route through shared typed/contextual family-step helpers while preserving the same ordered attempts, rejection aggregation, and `LoweringAttemptOutcome` behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the interval-family timer-counter IR assembly through one shared lowerer-owned semantic helper. `lower_interval_ir(...)` and `lower_interval_hold_ir(...)` no longer each own separate timer-backed counter builds; they now both route through one shared `lower_timed_counter_signal_ir(...)` family path while preserving the same node ids, sink/source ports, preview behavior, and subset-specific summed-vs-hold-on-tick output mode.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the interval-family parsed shape extraction through one shared lowerer-owned semantic helper. `lower_interval_contextual_attempt(...)` and `lower_interval_hold_contextual_attempt(...)` no longer each inline their own top-level binding fetch plus interval/document/counter shape validation; they now both route through one shared `lower_interval_signal_mode(...)` family path while preserving the same subset-specific validation rules, interval-ms extraction, and IR/view ids.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the interval-family contextual lowering shell through one shared lowerer-owned helper. `lower_interval_contextual_attempt(...)` and `lower_interval_hold_contextual_attempt(...)` no longer each open-code the same `lower_timer_backed_signal_surface(...)` wrapper around interval-mode parsing plus interval-mode IR selection; they now both route through one shared `lower_interval_signal_contextual_attempt(...)` family path while preserving the same labels, sink/source ports, root-binding behavior, and lowered program variants.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the timed-math action-tag and operation-choice IR assembly through shared lowerer-owned semantic helpers. `lower_hold_backed_timed_math_ir(...)` and `lower_while_ir(...)` no longer each open-code their own button-to-operation signal wiring, tag updates, and operation-choice mux assembly; they now both route through shared `append_timed_math_action_tags(...)`, `append_timed_math_operation_nodes(...)`, and `append_timed_math_operation_choice(...)` paths while preserving the same `Skip` fallback for the hold-backed `then`/`when` subsets and the same recompute-on-selection behavior for `while`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the hold-backed timed-flow typed-program wrapper through one shared lowerer-owned helper. `try_lower_then_from_expressions(...)` and `try_lower_when_from_expressions(...)` no longer each open-code their own `lower_timed_flow_program(...)` closure bodies around the same hold-backed timed-math base; they now both route through one shared `lower_hold_backed_timed_math_program(...)` path while preserving the same host-view base, sink/source ids, `Skip` fallback behavior, and optional subtraction-port requirement.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the hold-backed timed-math IR mode wrapper through one shared lowerer-owned helper. `lower_then_ir(...)` and `lower_when_ir(...)` no longer each exist as separate per-surface wrappers around `lower_hold_backed_timed_math_ir(...)`; both subsets now route through one shared `lower_hold_backed_timed_math_mode_ir(...)` path while preserving the same action sets, node-id bands, `Skip` fallback behavior, and subtraction-port requirement for `when`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the single-action counter accumulator program wrapper through one shared lowerer-owned helper. The `counter` surface no longer builds the same `CounterAccumulatorRuntimeConfig` twice for its `LATEST |> Math/sum()` and `HOLD` shapes; both branches now route through one shared `lower_single_action_counter_accumulator_program(...)` path while preserving the same press-port wiring, node ids, and hold-binding persistence behavior for the persistent `counter_hold` variant.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the contextual typed-program extraction shell through one shared lowerer-owned helper. The contextual typed entry points for `interval`, `interval_hold`, `fibonacci`, `layers`, `pages`, `latest`, `text_interpolation_update`, `while_function_call`, `button_hover_test`, and `switch_hold_test` no longer each open-code their own `lower_contextual_program(...)` plus “unexpected variant” wrapper; they now all route through one shared `lower_contextual_typed_program(...)` path while preserving the same per-surface contextual attempt functions and typed result variants.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the interval-family timed-counter IR mode wrapper through shared lowerer-owned config instead of separate per-surface functions. `lower_interval_ir(...)` and `lower_interval_hold_ir(...)` are gone; `lower_interval_contextual_attempt(...)` and `lower_interval_hold_contextual_attempt(...)` now carry `base_node_id` plus `TimedCounterOutputMode` directly in `IntervalSignalAttemptConfig`, and `lower_interval_signal_contextual_attempt(...)` routes both subsets through the shared `lower_timed_counter_signal_ir(...)` path while preserving the same node-id bands and summed-vs-held-on-tick behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the append-list ephemeral program finisher through one shared lowerer-owned helper. `list_retain_remove` and `shopping_list` no longer each end with their own identical `AppendListRuntime -> IrProgram { nodes, functions: Vec::new(), persistence: Vec::new() }` closure; both now route through one shared `lower_append_list_ephemeral_program(...)` path while preserving the same append-list runtime nodes, sink wiring, and non-persistent behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the timed-flow IR assembly itself through one shared lowerer-owned helper. The hold-backed `then` / `when` subsets and the live-selection `while` subset no longer bottom out in separate per-surface IR builders for the same “timed inputs, action tags, operation nodes, operation choice, and result sink” shape; they now all route through one shared `lower_timed_math_ir(...)` path, with shared input-hold and update-hold helpers controlling persistence-backed vs ephemeral inputs, latest-update vs held-selection action sources, and held-vs-direct result sinks while preserving the existing `then` / `when` `Skip` fallback behavior and the `while` recompute-on-selection semantics.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the direct source-backed hold field shape used by the form-runtime family. `temperature_converter` and `flight_booker` no longer each hand-roll the same “source port feeding a hold with a fixed seed” IR nodes inline for their editable store fields; both now route those fields through one shared `append_source_backed_hold(...)` helper while preserving the same node ids, seed values, ports, and downstream conversion/validation behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the common “merge updates with Latest, then retain through Hold” state-cell shape through one shared lowerer-owned helper. The append-list runtime, the counter accumulator runtime, the circle-drawer list runtime, and the timer resettable elapsed accumulator no longer each hand-roll their own inline `Latest { inputs: ... }` plus `Hold { seed, updates }` state cell assembly; they now route through one shared `append_latest_hold(...)` path while preserving the same node ids, single-vs-multi-update behavior for the counter accumulator, and reset/append/remove semantics for the other affected surfaces.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the common “append derived item into current list, optionally merge an alternate list update, then retain through Hold” list-state shape through one shared lowerer-owned helper. The append-list runtime and the circle-drawer runtime no longer each hand-roll their own `ListAppend` plus alternate-update plus `Latest`/`Hold` list-state assembly; they now route that shape through one shared `append_list_state_hold(...)` path while preserving the same node ids, clear/remove-last behavior, and retained list wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the common “source event triggers body value, optionally merged through Latest” update shape through one shared lowerer-owned helper. The temperature-converter edit-mode state, the timed-math action-tag wiring, and the counter accumulator runtime no longer each hand-roll their own inline `Then { source, body }` chains plus optional `Latest { inputs: ... }` merge; they now route that shape through one shared `append_source_triggered_updates(...)` path while preserving the same node ids, single-vs-multi-update behavior, and downstream hold semantics.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the common “source-triggered updates folded back into held state” shape through one shared lowerer-owned helper. The temperature-converter edit-mode state, the timer elapsed-state runtime, the accumulating timed-input helper used by the interval/timed-flow family, and the counter accumulator runtime no longer each hand-compose `append_source_triggered_updates(...)` plus `append_latest_hold(...)` or open-code equivalent `Then`/`Hold` state wiring; they now route that shape through one shared `append_source_triggered_hold(...)` path while preserving the same node ids, single-vs-multi-update behavior, and downstream sink/persistence semantics.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the raw seeded-hold cell assembly through shared lowerer-owned helpers. `append_source_backed_hold(...)`, `append_latest_hold(...)`, `append_hold_result_sink(...)`, and `append_updates_hold(...)` no longer each hand-roll their own `Hold { seed, updates }` plus optional sink nodes, and the remaining per-surface `flight_booker` booked-state hold plus `timer` duration-validation hold now route through the same `append_seeded_hold(...)` / `append_seeded_hold_sink(...)` path while preserving the same node ids, seeds, updates, and sink wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the common “source port selects one literal value into updates or held state” shape through shared lowerer-owned helpers. The `todo_mvc` selected-filter state no longer open-codes its three filter-port source/literal/then nodes plus `Latest`/`Hold`, and the timed-math action-tag builder no longer hand-rolls the same source-plus-literal staging before `append_source_triggered_updates(...)`; both now route through the shared `append_source_triggered_literal_updates(...)` / `append_source_triggered_literal_hold(...)` path while preserving the same node ids, literals, and held-selection behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the common “retain latest updates and immediately publish the held state” shape through one shared lowerer-owned helper. The remaining retained `todo_mvc` state cells for main-input text, edit target, edit draft, edit focus hint, edit focused, hovered target, and main-input focus hint no longer each hand-roll their own `Latest { inputs: ... }` or `Hold { seed, updates }` plus `SinkPort` boilerplate; they now route through the shared `append_latest_hold_sink(...)` / `append_seeded_hold_sink(...)` path while preserving the same node ids, seeds, updates, and sink wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes two more retained `todo_mvc` state cells through the same lowerer-owned hold/sink helpers. The main-input-focused state and the todos-list retained state no longer hand-roll their own `Hold { seed, updates }` / `Latest { inputs: ... }` plus `SinkPort` boilerplate; they now route through the shared `append_seeded_hold_sink(...)` / `append_latest_hold_sink(...)` path while preserving the same node ids, retained-list seed, update ordering, and sink wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes raw `Latest { inputs: ... }` merge construction through one shared lowerer-owned helper. `append_latest_hold(...)` and `append_source_triggered_updates(...)` no longer each own their own inline latest-merge shells, and the remaining open-coded `todo_mvc` latest merges for edit title, main-input focus state, hovered target state, and main-input focus-hint state now route through the shared `append_latest_inputs(...)` path while preserving the same node ids, input order, and latest-wins behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the common “source-triggered delta added back into a held accumulator” shape through one shared lowerer-owned helper. The timed-input accumulator path and the counter accumulator runtime no longer each hand-roll their own `SourcePort`, delta literal, `Add { lhs: hold, rhs: delta }`, and `append_source_triggered_hold(...)` assembly; they now route through the shared `append_source_delta_accumulator_hold(...)` path while preserving the same node ids, seed values, single-vs-multi-action merge behavior, and retained hold wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the common “source-triggered delta accumulator retained and immediately published to a sink” shape through one shared lowerer-owned helper. The timed-input accumulator path and the counter accumulator runtime no longer each route through `append_source_delta_accumulator_hold(...)` and then hand-emit a matching `SinkPort`; they now both route through the shared `append_source_delta_accumulator_hold_sink(...)` path while preserving the same node ids, zero-seed setup, sink wiring, and single-vs-multi-action merge behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the common “join text fragments and immediately publish the result” shape through one shared lowerer-owned helper. The append-list runtime, retained-count list runtime, timer display wiring, and circle-drawer count display no longer each hand-roll their own `TextJoin { inputs: ... }` plus matching `SinkPort`; they now route through the shared `append_text_join_sink(...)` path while preserving the same node ids, sink bindings, and rendered text order.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the common contextual “generic host surface plus labeled lowering” shell through shared lowerer-owned helpers. `text_interpolation_update`, `button_hover_test`, `while_function_call`, `switch_hold_test`, `layers`, `pages`, and `latest` no longer each hand-roll their own `lower_labeled_program(...)` wrapper around `lower_generic_host_surface_program(...)` or `lower_generic_host_surface_with_sink_values_program(...)`; they now route through shared contextual host-surface helpers while preserving the same structural validation, sink/source bindings, view sites, function instances, and typed program construction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining contextual “bindings-backed” and “timer-backed signal” labeled lowering shells through shared lowerer-owned helpers. `fibonacci` no longer hand-rolls its own `lower_labeled_program(...)` plus `lower_with_bindings(...)` wrapper around the sink-values-from-bindings host path, and `interval` / `interval_hold` no longer hand-roll their own `lower_labeled_program(...)` wrapper around `lower_timer_backed_signal_surface(...)`; they now route through shared contextual binding/timer helpers while preserving the same binding validation, sink values, interval extraction, node ids, and typed program construction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the common “single sink value derived from validated bindings” host-surface shell through one shared lowerer-owned helper. `fibonacci` and `static` no longer each hand-roll their own `lower_with_bindings(...)` or contextual binding wrapper around `lower_generic_host_surface_with_sink_values_from_bindings_program(...)` for one sink-backed display value; they now route through the shared `lower_bindings_single_sink_value_program(...)` path while preserving the same binding validation, sink ids, view sites, function instances, and rendered sink values.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the form-runtime family’s “IR already built, now attach the generic host IR surface” shell through one shared lowerer-owned helper. `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, and `timer` no longer each hand-roll their own final `GenericHostIrSurfaceConfig` plus `lower_generic_host_ir_program(...)` wrapper; they now route through the shared `lower_form_runtime_ir_program(...)` path while preserving the same structural validation, binding maps, view sites, function instances, timer-child wiring, and typed program construction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes `button_hover_to_click_test` through the shared contextual generic host-surface path. Its production contextual attempt no longer bounces back through the example-specific typed lowerer or the generic-host-IR surface wrapper; both the contextual and direct typed entry points now route through the same `lower_contextual_generic_host_surface_program(...)` path while preserving the same structural validation, sink/source bindings, view site, function instance, and typed program construction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the contextual “IR-backed generic host surface plus labeled lowering” shell through one shared lowerer-owned helper. `circle_drawer` no longer routes its production contextual attempt back through the example-specific typed lowerer, and its direct typed entry no longer carries a separate copy of the IR-plus-host-surface lowering shell; both now route through the shared `lower_contextual_generic_host_ir_program(...)` path while preserving the same structural validation, node ids, sink/source bindings, view site, function instance, and typed program construction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the checkbox-list host-surface family through one shared contextual lowerer-owned helper. `filter_checkbox_bug` and `checkbox_test` no longer route their production contextual attempts back through example-specific typed lowerers, and their direct typed entries no longer carry separate copies of the same checkbox-list host-surface shell; both subsets now route through the shared `lower_contextual_checkbox_list_surface_program(...)` path while preserving the same structural validation, mapped checkbox row wiring, view sites, function instances, sink/source ids, and typed program construction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the static-document bindings path through the shared contextual bindings helper. `static` no longer routes its production contextual attempt back through an example-specific typed wrapper, and its direct typed entry no longer carries a separate copy of the same bindings-plus-single-sink host-surface shell; both now route through `lower_contextual_with_bindings_program(...)` plus `lower_bindings_single_sink_value_program(...)` while preserving the same document-root extraction, sink id, view site, function instance, and rendered sink values.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the typed timed-math program shell through one shared lowerer-owned helper. `then`, `when`, and `while` no longer end in separate copies of the same “timed-flow base plus returned IR/host-view/ports/sinks bundle” assembly; they now route through the shared `lower_timed_math_program(...)` path while preserving the same timed-flow validation, timer/button/source wiring, hold-backed versus live-selection math semantics, and typed program construction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes `chained_list_remove_bug` through the shared contextual checkbox-list host-surface path. Its production lowering no longer routes through the typed list family entry or carries a separate direct `lower_checkbox_list_surface_program(...)` shell; both the contextual family attempt and the direct typed entry now route through `lower_chained_list_remove_bug_contextual_attempt(...)` and the shared `lower_contextual_checkbox_list_surface_program(...)` helper while preserving the same structural validation, mapped checkbox row wiring, action-button ports, title/count sinks, and typed program construction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the flat-stripe list display family through shared contextual lowerer-owned helpers. `list_map_external_dep`, `list_map_block`, and `list_object_state` no longer route their direct typed entries through separate `lower_flat_stripe_surface_program(...)` or `lower_flat_stripe_host_only_surface_program(...)` production shells; they now route through contextual attempts built on `lower_contextual_flat_stripe_surface_program(...)` and `lower_contextual_flat_stripe_host_only_surface_program(...)` while preserving the same structural validation, static retained HostView wiring, sink/source ids, and typed program construction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the append-list surface family through one shared contextual lowerer-owned helper and a shared contextual-first family step. `list_retain_count`, `list_retain_remove`, and `shopping_list` no longer route their direct typed entries or list-family production path through separate `lower_append_list_surface_program(...)` shells; they now route through contextual attempts built on `lower_contextual_append_list_surface_program(...)`, and the list family now tries those shared contextual attempts before falling back to the remaining typed-only list subsets. This preserves the same append-list runtime wiring, retained HostView shape, sink/source ids, and typed program construction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the titled-column CRUD family through the shared contextual lowerer-owned helper and contextual-first list-family step. `crud` no longer routes its direct typed entry or list-family production path through a separate `lower_titled_column_surface_program(...)` shell; both now route through `lower_crud_contextual_attempt(...)` and `lower_contextual_titled_column_surface_program(...)` while preserving the same structural validation, row-slot wiring, form/button ports, sink ids, and typed program construction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the counter family through shared contextual lowerer-owned helpers. `counter` no longer routes its direct typed entry or family production path through a separate bindings-plus-generic-host-IR shell, `complex_counter` no longer routes through a separate direct generic-host-IR shell, and the counter family no longer falls back to typed attempts; both subsets now route through `lower_counter_contextual_attempt(...)`, `lower_complex_counter_contextual_attempt(...)`, `lower_contextual_bindings_with_generic_host_ir_program(...)`, and the contextual-only `COUNTER_CONTEXTUAL_ATTEMPTS` family step while preserving the same press-port extraction, accumulator runtime wiring, hover mirrors, sink/source ids, and typed program construction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining reactive flat-stripe list path through a shared contextual bindings helper. `list_retain_reactive` no longer routes its direct typed entry or list-family production path through a separate bindings-plus-`lower_flat_stripe_surface_program_from_bindings(...)` shell; it now routes through `lower_list_retain_reactive_contextual_attempt(...)`, `lower_contextual_bindings_with_flat_stripe_surface_program(...)`, and the contextual-first `LIST_CONTEXTUAL_ATTEMPTS` step, while the list typed fallback shrinks to the still-separate `todo_mvc` path. This preserves the same retained filter-toggle IR, durable hold persistence, flat-stripe HostView shape, sink/source ids, and typed program construction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the form-runtime family through shared contextual family dispatch. `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, and `timer` no longer route their production family path through typed attempts; they now route through `lower_temperature_converter_contextual_attempt(...)`, `lower_flight_booker_contextual_attempt(...)`, `lower_timer_contextual_attempt(...)`, the shared `FORM_RUNTIME_CONTEXTUAL_ATTEMPTS` set, and the contextual `lower_form_runtime_family_step(...)`, while preserving the same already-shared `lower_form_runtime_ir_program(...)` lowering shell, sink/source ids, retained HostView shape, and typed program construction.
