- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the timed-flow family through shared contextual family dispatch. `then`, `when`, and `while` no longer route their production family path through typed attempt tables; they now route through `lower_then_contextual_attempt(...)`, `lower_when_contextual_attempt(...)`, `lower_while_contextual_attempt(...)`, the shared `TIMED_FLOW_CONTEXTUAL_ATTEMPTS` set, and the contextual `lower_timed_flow_family_step(...)`, while preserving the same already-shared `lower_timed_math_program(...)` and `lower_hold_backed_timed_math_program(...)` lowering shells, timed button/tick wiring, sink/source ids, and typed program construction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the shared contextual expression shell that still sat beneath several shipped families. `cells`, the form-runtime trio, and the timed-flow trio no longer each open-code their own `lower_labeled_program(...)` plus `try_lower_*_from_expressions(...)` adapter; they now route through one shared `lower_contextual_expression_program(...)` helper, and the old dead `lower_typed_expression_program(...)` shim is gone. This preserves the same subset labeling, typed program construction, and direct typed-entry behavior while removing another per-surface lowering shell from the production path.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the repeated direct typed-entry contextual-variant shell. The contextual-only shipped families no longer each open-code the same `lower_contextual_typed_program(...)` plus `match LoweredProgram::{Variant}` adapter for `counter`, `todo_mvc`, `complex_counter`, `list_retain_reactive`, `chained_list_remove_bug`, `crud`, `interval`, `interval_hold`, `fibonacci`, `layers`, `pages`, `latest`, `while_function_call`, `button_hover_to_click_test`, `button_hover_test`, `switch_hold_test`, `circle_drawer`, and `static`; they now route through one shared `lower_contextual_variant_program!` helper while preserving the same direct typed-entry behavior and variant extraction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining single hold-binding persistence-spec shell. `list_retain_reactive` and the single-action `counter` accumulator no longer each hand-build their own one-element hold-binding spec collections; they now route through the shared `single_hold_binding_persistence_specs(...)` helper, and `lower_counter_accumulator_program(...)` now accepts any persistence-spec iterator instead of forcing a per-surface `Vec`. This preserves the same durable hold metadata while moving another persistence decision away from per-surface ad hoc assembly.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the last remaining list/toggle direct typed-entry adapters that were still bypassing the shared variant helper. `list_map_external_dep`, `list_map_block`, `list_retain_count`, `list_object_state`, `list_retain_remove`, `shopping_list`, `filter_checkbox_bug`, `checkbox_test`, and `text_interpolation_update` no longer each open-code their own `lower_contextual_typed_program(...)` plus `match LoweredProgram::{Variant}` wrapper; they now route through the same shared `lower_contextual_variant_program!` helper as the other contextual-only shipped subsets, preserving the same direct typed-entry behavior and variant extraction while removing another block of per-surface lowering shell code.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the last interval-family subset wrapper layer through shared config-driven dispatch. The `interval` and `interval_hold` production family step no longer routes through separate `lower_interval_contextual_attempt(...)` / `lower_interval_hold_contextual_attempt(...)` wrappers, and the direct typed entry points no longer depend on those wrapper functions either; both now route through shared `INTERVAL_*_SIGNAL_CONFIG` constants, the shared `lower_interval_signal_contextual_attempt(...)` path, and the new closure-capable `lower_contextual_program_with(...)` helper while preserving the same subset order, node-id bands, timer ports, root-binding behavior, and variant extraction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the last bespoke single-path persistence collection shell. `todo_mvc` and the hold-backed timed-input helper no longer route through separate `collect_list_store_path_persistence(...)` / `collect_hold_path_persistence(...)` wrappers; both now use the shared `collect_single_lowering_persistence(...)` path together with the existing `list_store_path_persistence_spec(...)` / `hold_path_persistence_spec(...)` constructors, preserving the same durable todo-list and timed-input hold metadata while removing another bit of per-surface persistence helper selection.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining one-spec persistence array shell. `todo_mvc`, the hold-backed timed-input helper, `list_retain_reactive`, and the single-action `counter` accumulator no longer split between `collect_single_lowering_persistence(...)` and `single_hold_binding_persistence_specs(...)`; all four now route through one shared `single_lowering_persistence_specs(...)` helper together with the existing spec constructors, preserving the same durable hold/list-store metadata while removing another per-surface distinction from the persistence derivation path.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the form-runtime and timed-flow contextual expression family shells through shared config-driven dispatch. `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, `timer`, `then`, `when`, and `while` no longer route their production family path through private `lower_*_contextual_attempt(...)` wrappers; both families now use shared `ContextualExpressionAttemptConfig` tables plus `lower_contextual_expression_attempt(...)` / `lower_contextual_expression_family_program(...)`, while the per-subset typed lowerers are adapted through shared `define_lowered_expression_program!` wrappers that preserve the same typed parsing, variant wrapping, and family ordering.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the non-interval family runner itself through one shared attempt enum and dispatcher. The counter, toggle-local-state, list, display, form-runtime, and timed-flow family steps no longer split between separate contextual-only and expression-only loop helpers; they now all route through one shared `FamilyAttempt` enum plus `run_family_attempts(...)` / `lower_family_program(...)`, and the display family now carries `cells` through that same mixed attempt path instead of keeping a final one-off `lower_cells_contextual_attempt(...)` wrapper or the now-removed `lower_contextual_expression_program(...)` helper.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the last bespoke interval-family family-step shell. `interval` and `interval_hold` no longer keep a private production loop over `INTERVAL_SIGNAL_ATTEMPT_CONFIGS`, and their direct typed entries no longer open-code closure-based contextual variant extraction; both subsets now route through the shared `FamilyAttempt` / `lower_family_program(...)` path, the new shared `lower_contextual_expression_program_with(...)` helper, and the new shared `lower_contextual_variant_program_with!` helper while preserving the same interval configs, ordering, timer ports, and variant extraction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the repeated generic-host-surface contextual-attempt shell for the remaining toggle/display subsets that still used it directly. `text_interpolation_update`, `button_hover_to_click_test`, `button_hover_test`, `while_function_call`, `switch_hold_test`, `pages`, and `latest` no longer each hand-write the same local `GenericHostSurfaceConfig` binding plus `lower_contextual_generic_host_surface_program(...)` wrapper; they now route through one shared `define_generic_host_surface_contextual_attempt!` macro while preserving the same validation specs, port bindings, sink bindings, function/view ids, and typed program assembly.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the repeated checkbox-list contextual-attempt shell. `filter_checkbox_bug`, `checkbox_test`, and `chained_list_remove_bug` no longer each hand-write the same local `CheckboxListSurfaceConfig` binding plus `lower_contextual_checkbox_list_surface_program(...)` wrapper; they now route through one shared `define_checkbox_list_contextual_attempt!` macro while preserving the same validation specs, checkbox-row configs, prefix/suffix layout, port bindings, sink bindings, and typed program assembly.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the repeated append-list contextual-attempt shell. `list_retain_count`, `list_retain_remove`, and `shopping_list` no longer each hand-write the same local `AppendListSurfaceConfig` binding plus `lower_contextual_append_list_surface_program(...)` wrapper; they now route through one shared `define_append_list_contextual_attempt!` macro while preserving the same validation specs, runtime configs, host-view configs, IR builders, port bindings, sink bindings, and typed program assembly.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the repeated host-only flat-stripe contextual-attempt shell. `list_map_block` and `list_object_state` no longer each hand-write the same local `FlatStripeHostOnlySurfaceConfig` plus `lower_contextual_flat_stripe_host_only_surface_program(...)` wrapper; they now route through one shared `define_flat_stripe_host_only_contextual_attempt!` macro while preserving the same validation specs, document configs, mapped-row configs, port bindings, sink bindings, and typed program assembly.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the repeated generic-host-IR contextual-attempt shell. `circle_drawer` and `complex_counter` no longer each hand-write the same local `GenericHostIrSurfaceConfig` binding plus `lower_contextual_generic_host_ir_program(...)` wrapper; they now route through one shared `define_generic_host_ir_contextual_attempt!` macro while preserving the same validation specs, IR builders, port bindings, sink bindings, timer-child config, function/view ids, and typed program assembly.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the repeated bindings-to-single-sink contextual shell. `fibonacci` and `static` no longer each hand-write the same `lower_contextual_with_bindings_program(...)` plus `lower_bindings_single_sink_value_program(...)` wrapper; they now route through one shared `lower_contextual_bindings_single_sink_value_program(...)` helper while preserving the same top-level binding validation, sink binding names, view/function ids, host-view lowering, and final sink values.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining flat-stripe list-surface contextual shell that still split fixed-IR and bindings-derived-IR paths. `list_map_external_dep` and `list_retain_reactive` no longer route through separate `lower_contextual_flat_stripe_surface_program(...)` vs `lower_contextual_bindings_with_flat_stripe_surface_program(...)` wrappers; both now share one `define_bindings_with_flat_stripe_contextual_attempt!` macro and the same validated-bindings flat-stripe lowering path, while preserving the same validation specs, document configs, IR builders, port bindings, sink bindings, and typed program assembly.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining one-spec persistence-array shells. `todo_mvc`, the hold-backed timed-input helper, `list_retain_reactive`, and the hold-binding single-action counter path no longer each spell out `single_lowering_persistence_specs(…_persistence_spec(...))` directly at the call site; they now route through shared `single_list_store_path_persistence_specs(...)`, `single_hold_path_persistence_specs(...)`, and `single_hold_binding_persistence_specs(...)` helpers while preserving the same durable hold/list-store metadata and reducing one more per-surface persistence-shape distinction.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining bindings-to-single-sink contextual attempt wrappers themselves. `fibonacci` and `static` no longer each hand-write their own local `lower_contextual_bindings_single_sink_value_program(...)` call plus typed-program assembly; they now route through one shared `define_bindings_single_sink_value_contextual_attempt!` macro while preserving the same binding validation, sink binding names, view/function ids, host-view lowering, and final sink-value derivation closures.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes four more one-off contextual wrapper shells that were still sitting outside the shared lowering spine. `todo_mvc`, `crud`, `layers`, and `counter` no longer each hand-write their own local `lower_contextual_template_backed_ir_surface_program(...)`, `lower_contextual_titled_column_surface_program(...)`, `lower_contextual_generic_host_surface_with_sink_values_program(...)`, or `lower_contextual_bindings_with_generic_host_ir_program(...)` wrapper function; they now route through shared `define_template_backed_ir_contextual_attempt!`, `define_titled_column_contextual_attempt!`, `define_generic_host_surface_with_sink_values_contextual_attempt!`, and `define_bindings_with_generic_host_ir_contextual_attempt!` macros while preserving the same validation specs, IR builders, sink/source bindings, host-view configs, typed program assembly, and persistence derivation.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining interval-family timer-backed wrapper layer. `interval` and `interval_hold` no longer route through the bespoke `lower_interval_signal_contextual_attempt(...)` function plus dedicated expression-program adapters; they now route through shared `define_timer_backed_signal_contextual_attempt!` contextual attempts and the ordinary contextual typed-entry path while preserving the same timer-backed signal config, output mode, host-view bindings, tick source, and timed-counter IR assembly.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also collapses the family dispatcher onto one top-level attempt kind. `cells`, `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, `timer`, `then`, `when`, and `while` no longer require `FamilyAttempt::Expression`, `ContextualExpressionAttemptConfig`, `lower_contextual_expression_attempt(...)`, and `define_lowered_expression_program!` just to reach the ordered family pipeline; they now route through shared `define_expression_contextual_attempt!` contextual attempts, and `run_family_attempts(...)` now dispatches one contextual-attempt shape across the counter, interval, toggle, list, display, form-runtime, and timed-flow families.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the repetitive typed contextual entrypoint pair. The contextual subsets that already shared `lower_contextual_variant_program!(...)` no longer each hand-write both `pub fn try_lower_*` and matching `fn try_lower_*_from_expressions(...)` wrappers; they now route through one shared `define_contextual_variant_entrypoint!` macro while preserving the same parse step, typed return programs, contextual attempt routing, and subset/variant checks for counter, todo_mvc, complex_counter, reactive/list CRUD variants, interval variants, display variants, toggle variants, and static-document entrypoints.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the direct timed-flow semantic entry configurations. `then`, `when`, and `while` no longer each hand-build a full inline `TimedFlowProgramConfig` plus their final typed-program field projection inside `try_lower_*_from_expressions(...)`; they now share `THEN_TIMED_FLOW_CONFIG`, `WHEN_TIMED_FLOW_CONFIG`, `WHILE_TIMED_FLOW_CONFIG`, and shared `TimedMathProgramLowering::{into_then_program,into_when_program,into_while_program}` conversions while preserving the same validation gates, timer/button ports, sink wiring, and timed-math IR behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the direct form-runtime semantic entry configurations. `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, and `timer` no longer each hand-build a full inline validation/sink/source/timer shell plus their final typed-program field projection inside `try_lower_*_from_expressions(...)`; they now share `TEMPERATURE_CONVERTER_FORM_RUNTIME_CONFIG`, `FLIGHT_BOOKER_FORM_RUNTIME_CONFIG`, `TIMER_FORM_RUNTIME_CONFIG`, the shared `lower_form_runtime_program(...)` entry, and shared `FormRuntimeProgramLowering::{into_temperature_converter_program,into_flight_booker_program,into_timer_program}` conversions while preserving the same validation gates, control ports, sink wiring, timer-child config, and IR behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining direct source-parse entry shell across both contextual and manual typed families. The public typed entrypoints no longer split between hand-written `parse_static_expressions(source)?` wrappers for `todo_mvc_physical`, `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, `timer`, `then`, `when`, and `while` versus the contextual-only `define_contextual_variant_entrypoint!` path; they now all route through one shared `define_source_parsed_entrypoint!` macro while preserving the same private `*_from_expressions(...)` lowering functions and typed results.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the toggle-selected-list semantic entry shell that still split the last config/value assembly between `list_retain_reactive` and `list_map_external_dep`. Those two surfaces no longer hand-wire their final bool-toggle runtime config, item-list sink, auxiliary text/count sink, and selected-list values separately right before calling `lower_toggle_selected_list_ir(...)`; they now share `ToggleSelectedListProgramConfig`, `ToggleSelectedListValues`, the shared `lower_toggle_selected_list_program(...)` entry, and the `LIST_RETAIN_REACTIVE_TOGGLE_CONFIG` / `LIST_MAP_EXTERNAL_DEP_TOGGLE_CONFIG` configs while preserving the same binding-derived vs static item values, persistence, ports, sinks, and IR behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the toggle-selected-list semantic IR builder itself. `list_retain_reactive` and `list_map_external_dep` no longer split between separate top-level semantic builders that manually unpack bindings vs static values before invoking the shared toggle runtime; they now share `ToggleSelectedListSemanticConfig`, `ToggleSelectedListSemanticMode`, and `lower_toggle_selected_list_semantic_ir(...)`, while the reactive path keeps its binding-derived retained integer extraction and persistence metadata and the external-dependency path keeps its static string lists through the same lowerer-owned semantic entry.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the last two per-surface toggle-selected-list semantic entry functions from the production path. The contextual attempts for `list_retain_reactive` and `list_map_external_dep` no longer bounce through `lower_list_retain_reactive_ir(...)` or `lower_list_map_external_dep_ir()` before reaching the shared semantic IR builder; both now call `lower_toggle_selected_list_semantic_ir(...)` directly with their shared semantic configs, leaving the family on one lowerer-owned semantic entry instead of surface-specific trampoline functions.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining inline `todo_mvc` persistence/semantic entry shell. The `todo_mvc` contextual attempt no longer hand-builds `collect_lowering_persistence(...)` plus `single_list_store_path_persistence_specs(...)` inline before dropping into `lower_todo_ui_state_ir(...)`; it now routes through `TODO_MVC_SEMANTIC_CONFIG` and the shared `lower_todo_ui_state_semantic_ir(...)` helper, keeping the `store.todos` list-store persistence path, hold node, and local slot in one lowerer-owned semantic config instead of a per-surface closure body.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining inline `todo_mvc` template-materialization shell. The `todo_mvc` production path and `TodoProgram::materialize_host_view(...)` no longer route through a dedicated `materialize_todo_host_view_from_sink_values(...)` function; they now use the shared `materialize_host_view_from_derived_sink_values(...)` helper together with the existing todo-specific sink-derivation function and template, keeping the derived-sink template materialization pattern lowerer-owned instead of per-surface.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining template-backed “derived sink values plus template” lowering shell. `todo_mvc` no longer reaches production lowering through `define_template_backed_ir_contextual_attempt!` plus an inline derived-sink materializer closure; it now routes through the shared `lower_template_backed_derived_sink_surface(...)`, `lower_template_backed_derived_sink_surface_program(...)`, `lower_contextual_template_backed_derived_sink_surface_program(...)`, and `define_template_backed_derived_sink_contextual_attempt!` path while preserving the same `todo_host_view_sink_values(...)`, `todo_host_view_template()`, IR builder, and typed program assembly.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining hand-written “lower shared family object, then convert to typed program” direct-entry shell. `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, `timer`, `then`, `when`, and `while` no longer each spell out that conversion pattern directly after their shared form-runtime / timed-math lowerers; they now route through shared `lower_form_runtime_variant_program(...)` and `lower_timed_math_variant_program(...)` helpers while preserving the same IR construction, family configs, and typed result conversions.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the parallel direct-entry route for the shared form-runtime and timed-flow subsets. `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, `timer`, `then`, `when`, and `while` no longer publish their typed `try_lower_*` APIs through standalone `define_source_parsed_entrypoint!` wrappers that bypass the contextual spine; they now use `define_contextual_variant_entrypoint!` like the other shared subsets, while the actual family builders remain private `lower_*_program_from_expressions(...)` helpers used by the contextual attempts.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining single-spec persistence collection shells that already terminate in collected persistence entries. The `todo_mvc` list-store persistence path, hold-backed timed-input helper, and counter accumulator optional persistence path no longer each spell out their own `collect_lowering_persistence(...)` or `bindings.map_or_else(...)` pattern around the shared single-spec helpers; they now route through shared `collect_single_list_store_path_lowering_persistence(...)`, `collect_single_hold_path_lowering_persistence(...)`, and `collect_optional_lowering_persistence(...)` helpers while preserving the same durable metadata and IR behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining toggle-selected-list persistence handoff inside the shared semantic lowerer. The reactive toggle-selected-list path no longer threads raw `LoweringPersistenceSpec`s down through `lower_toggle_selected_list_program(...)` and `lower_bool_toggle_runtime(...)`; `lower_toggle_selected_list_semantic_ir(...)` now derives final durable metadata through `collect_single_hold_path_lowering_persistence(...)`, and the shared toggle runtime consumes finished `IrNodePersistence` directly while preserving the same retained bool-toggle behavior and sinks for both `list_retain_reactive` and `list_map_external_dep`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining single-action counter persistence handoff inside the shared accumulator lowerer. The hold-backed counter path no longer threads raw hold-binding `LoweringPersistenceSpec`s or an optional bindings wrapper through `lower_counter_accumulator_program(...)`; it now derives final durable metadata through `collect_single_hold_binding_lowering_persistence(...)`, and the shared accumulator lowerer consumes finished `IrNodePersistence` directly while preserving the same counter IR and mirror-sink behavior for both `counter` and `complex_counter`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the dead generic persistence-spec classifier layer that was only serving the old path-based handoff. Path-derived persistence no longer routes through `LoweringPersistenceSource`, `LoweringPersistenceSpec`, and `collect_lowering_persistence(...)`; it now goes straight through the shared direct collectors for binding and path persistence, while the shared persistence-helper coverage still exercises the same hold/list-store durable metadata behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining template-backed derived HostView wiring for `todo_mvc`. The production contextual lowerer and `TodoProgram` no longer each thread `todo_host_view_sink_values(...)` and `todo_host_view_template()` separately through the shared template-backed derived-sink path; they now share one `TemplateBackedDerivedSinkHostViewConfig` object that owns both the sink-derivation function and template materialization while preserving the same derived `VISIBLE_TODOS` / active-count host-view behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the repeated source-triggered update chains that still dominated the remaining `todo_mvc` semantic lowering block. The edit-target, edit-draft, edit-focus-hint, and edit-focused state paths no longer each hand-emit their own parallel `IrNodeKind::Then { source, body }` chains before feeding `append_latest_hold_sink(...)`; they now route through one shared `TriggeredUpdateConfig` plus `append_triggered_updates(...)` helper while preserving the same state transitions and sink behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes three more retained `todo_mvc` state cells through the shared triggered-update hold/sink helper. The main-input-focused, hovered-target, and main-input-focus-hint states no longer hand-emit their own `Then { source, body }` node bands before separately feeding `append_latest_inputs(...)` and `append_seeded_hold_sink(...)`; they now route through `append_latest_hold_sink_with_triggered_updates(...)` while preserving the same seeds, node ids, update ordering, and sink wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining edit-session retained `todo_mvc` state cells through that same shared triggered-update hold/sink helper. The edit-target, edit-draft, edit-focus-hint, and edit-focused states no longer build `append_triggered_updates(...)` results in local variables before separately routing them into `append_latest_hold_sink(...)`; they now all route directly through `append_latest_hold_sink_with_triggered_updates(...)` while preserving the same seeds, base updates, node ids, and sink wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the retained `todo_mvc` todos-list state through that same shared triggered-update hold/sink helper. The production path no longer hand-emits the five source-triggered `Then { source, body }` wrappers for toggle, toggle-all, clear-completed, edit-commit, and delete before feeding the retained list into `append_latest_hold_sink(...)`; it now routes the list seed, submit-path base update, and those triggered updates through `append_latest_hold_sink_with_triggered_updates(...)` while preserving the same node ids, update ordering, persistence metadata, and sink wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the retained `todo_mvc` main-input text state through that same shared triggered-update hold/sink helper. The production path no longer hand-emits a separate submit-to-empty-string `Then { source, body }` node before routing the main-input draft mirror and change source through `append_latest_hold_sink(...)`; it now routes the draft mirror, change source, and submit clear action directly through `append_latest_hold_sink_with_triggered_updates(...)` while preserving the same seed, node ids, update ordering, and sink wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the retained `todo_mvc` selected-filter state through a shared source-triggered hold/sink helper. The production path no longer routes the three filter-button source/literal updates through `append_source_triggered_literal_hold(...)` and then hand-emits a separate `SinkPort`; it now routes the same seed, source/literal configs, node ids, and sink wiring through one shared `append_source_triggered_literal_hold_sink(...)` helper.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the repeated “derive list summary value, then immediately sink it” shell through shared lowerer-owned helpers. The `todo_mvc` active-count, completed-count, and all-completed summary outputs no longer each hand-emit their own `ListCount` or `ListAllObjectBoolField` node plus matching `SinkPort`; they now route through `append_list_count_sink(...)` and `append_list_all_object_bool_field_sink(...)` while preserving the same node ids, list inputs, and sink wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the shared edit-focus follow-up updates in `todo_mvc` through the generic triggered-update helper. The production path no longer hand-emits the `TODO_EDIT_FOCUS_PORT -> false`, `TODO_EDIT_BLUR_PORT -> false`, and `TODO_EDIT_FOCUS_PORT -> true` `Then { source, body }` nodes before reusing them as base updates for the edit-focus-hint and edit-focused retained cells; it now derives those same node ids through `append_triggered_updates(...)` and reuses the returned shared updates.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the repeated “count a list, prefix it, then sink it” tail through a shared helper. The generic toggle-selected-list family no longer hand-emits separate `ListCount`, prefix-literal, `TextJoin`, and `SinkPort` tails for `CountText`, the static-text branch no longer hand-emits its own literal `SinkPort`, and the append-list retain-count runtime no longer open-codes the same prefixed count shell; they now route through shared `append_prefixed_list_count_sink(...)` and `append_value_sink(...)` helpers while preserving the same node ids, inputs, and sink wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the append-list family’s generic sink tails through shared helpers. `lower_append_list_runtime(...)` no longer hand-emits its title sink, input sink, items-list sink, or the decorated count label shell; it now routes those through shared `append_value_sink(...)` and `append_decorated_list_count_sink(...)`, which also lets the count-label path cover both prefixed and suffixed variants without open-coded per-family wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining `circle_drawer` output tail through those same shared helpers. The production lowerer no longer hand-emits its title `SinkPort`, circles-list `SinkPort`, or the prefixed circles-count `TextJoin` shell; it now routes the same node ids and sink wiring through shared `append_value_sink(...)` and `append_prefixed_list_count_sink(...)`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the shared form-runtime family’s direct sink batches through `append_value_sink(...)`. The direct `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, and `timer` lowerers no longer hand-emit their repeated “existing value node to `SinkPort`” tails for titles, mirrored/held values, and static labels; they now route those same node ids and sink ids through one shared sink helper, leaving the family-specific logic focused on the semantic nodes instead of bespoke output wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the shared form-runtime family’s literal-to-sink shells through `append_literal_sink(...)`. The direct `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, and `timer` lowerers no longer hand-emit literal nodes that exist only to be immediately sunk as titles or static labels; those now route through one shared literal-plus-sink helper while preserving the same node ids and sink wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the shared timed-math / timed-counter family’s direct sink tails through `append_value_sink(...)`. The timed-math direct-result path, both `TimedCounterOutputMode` branches, and the counter-accumulator mirror sink loop no longer hand-emit standalone `SinkPort` nodes for already-computed values; they now route those same node ids and sink ids through the shared sink helper.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the shared bool-toggle and delta-accumulator helper sink tails through `append_value_sink(...)`. The `lower_bool_toggle_runtime(...)` mode-label output and `append_source_delta_accumulator_hold_sink(...)` no longer hand-emit standalone `SinkPort` nodes for already-computed values; they now route those same node ids and sink ids through the shared sink helper.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining shared seeded-hold and text-join helper sink tails through `append_value_sink(...)`. `append_seeded_hold_sink(...)` and `append_text_join_sink(...)` no longer hand-emit standalone `SinkPort` nodes for already-computed values, leaving `append_value_sink(...)` as the one shared sink-emission point for those helper paths.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the repeated trimmed-non-empty todo gating pattern through shared helpers. The `todo_mvc` create and edit-commit semantic paths no longer each hand-build their own `TextTrim` plus `Eq` plus `When(true => Skip, fallback => value)` chains; they now route through shared `append_trimmed_text(...)` and `append_non_empty_value_or_skip(...)` helpers while preserving the same node ids and skip semantics.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes repeated event-payload field extraction through shared helpers. The `todo_mvc` edit-commit, delete, and begin-edit paths and the `circle_drawer` canvas-click path no longer hand-build their local `SourcePort` plus `FieldRead` chains for `id` / `title` / `x` / `y`; they now route through shared `append_source_port(...)` and `append_field_read(...)` helpers while preserving the same node ids and event wiring.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the form-runtime family’s repeated source-backed input hold setup through a shared batch helper. The direct `temperature_converter` and `flight_booker` lowerers no longer each hand-instantiate their repeated `append_source_backed_hold(...)` sequences; they now route those same seeds, ports, node ids, and hold ids through shared `SourceBackedHoldConfig` plus `append_source_backed_holds(...)`, keeping that repeated input-state shell in the lowerer-owned helper layer instead of per-surface code.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes source-port-triggered update setup through shared helpers. The direct `flight_booker` and `timer` lowerers no longer hand-build their local `SourcePort` plus `Then` shells for book/tick/reset updates; they now route those same source ports, body nodes, source ids, and then ids through shared `SourcePortTriggeredBodyConfig`, `append_source_port_triggered_updates(...)`, and `append_source_port_triggered_hold(...)`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also broadens shared triggered-update wiring outside the form-runtime family. The shared append-list runtime no longer hand-builds its clear-list `SourcePort` plus `Then` shell; it now routes that update through `SourcePortTriggeredBodyConfig` plus `append_source_port_triggered_updates(...)`, while `circle_drawer` now reuses the generic `append_triggered_updates(...)` helper for its draw-circle `Then` node instead of open-coding that node inline.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the timed-flow family’s remaining direct lowering wrappers through one shared variant helper. The direct `then`, `when`, and `while` lowerers no longer each carry their own custom lowering closure around hold-backed vs direct timed-math setup; they now route through shared `TimedFlowVariantLoweringMode` plus `lower_timed_flow_variant_program(...)`, leaving the per-surface entries as config-plus-converter selections instead of bespoke wrapper logic.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes more of `todo_mvc`’s remaining event-source plumbing through the shared lowerer helpers. The production `todo_mvc` semantic lowerer no longer hand-builds raw `SourcePort` nodes for main-input change/key-down, hover/toggle, toggle-all, clear-completed, edit-change/cancel, and focus/blur ports, and it no longer hand-builds the hover/toggle `FieldRead` ids; those now route through shared `append_source_port(...)` and `append_field_read(...)`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining duplicated Enter-key gate shape that was still split between `todo_mvc` and the shared append-list runtime. The `todo_mvc` main-input submit path no longer hand-builds `KeyDownKey -> Literal(\"Enter\") -> Eq -> When`, and `lower_append_list_runtime(...)` no longer open-codes a separate `KeyDownKey -> When(\"Enter\")` chain; both now route through shared `append_key_down_match(...)`, preserving the same source ports, submit behavior, and lowered output while removing two more per-surface semantic shells.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also routes the remaining stray raw event helper bypasses through the shared lowerer-owned helper layer. The `todo_mvc` hovered-delete-button path no longer hand-builds its last direct `FieldRead`, `circle_drawer` no longer hand-builds the undo `SourcePort`, `timer` no longer hand-builds the duration-slider `SourcePort`, and the timed-counter summed-updates branch no longer hand-builds the tick `SourcePort`; those now route through shared `append_field_read(...)` / `append_source_port(...)`, leaving the production path with fewer one-off source/field node emissions outside the helper layer while preserving the same node ids and behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining raw source-node emission shells beneath the shared helper layer. The shared bool-toggle runtime, source-backed hold helper, source-triggered literal helper, source-delta accumulator helper, and append-list runtime no longer hand-emit raw `SourcePort` nodes at their own call sites; they now all route through `append_source_port(...)`, and `rg` now shows the single remaining `IrNodeKind::SourcePort(...)` site only inside that helper itself.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining raw triggered-update and list-summary node shells beneath the shared helper layer. The shared bool-toggle runtime, append-list runtime, timed-counter output builder, `todo_mvc` toggle-all path, and the summary/count sink helpers no longer hand-emit raw `Then`, `ListCount`, or `ListAllObjectBoolField` nodes at their own call sites; they now route through shared `append_then(...)`, `append_list_count(...)`, and `append_list_all_object_bool_field(...)`, and `rg` now shows those node kinds only inside the helper primitives themselves.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining raw trim/non-empty and non-sink text-join shells beneath the shared helper layer. The append-list family no longer hand-builds its `TextTrim` plus empty-string gating nodes, and `flight_booker` no longer hand-builds its two intermediate booking-message `TextJoin` nodes; they now route through shared `append_trimmed_text(...)`, `append_non_empty_value_or_skip(...)`, and `append_text_join(...)`, and `rg` now shows `IrNodeKind::TextTrim` / `IrNodeKind::TextJoin` only inside those helper primitives.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining raw conditional node shells beneath the shared helper layer. The shared bool-toggle runtime, keydown matcher, non-empty gate, toggle-selected-list helper, `todo_mvc` edit-focus/hover helpers, and `flight_booker` booking-message selector no longer hand-build raw `When` nodes at their own call sites; they now route through shared `append_when(...)`, and `rg` now shows `IrNodeKind::When` only inside that helper plus one test assertion.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes most of the remaining raw state-selection `While` shells beneath the shared helper layer. The direct `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, and `timer` lowerers no longer hand-build their repeated `While` nodes for mode selection, booking-state selection, and validated slider fallback; they now route those through shared `append_while(...)`, and `rg` now shows `IrNodeKind::While` only inside that shared helper plus the pre-existing shared timed-math operation-choice helper.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining raw `BoolNot` helper bypasses and the last timed-math `While` bypass beneath the shared helper layer. The bool-toggle runtime and `todo_mvc` toggle-all path no longer hand-build raw `BoolNot` nodes, and `append_timed_math_operation_choice(...)` no longer hand-builds its own raw `While`; they now route through shared `append_bool_not(...)` and `append_while(...)`, and `rg` now shows `IrNodeKind::BoolNot` / `IrNodeKind::While` only inside the shared helper primitives.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining raw mirror-cell helper bypasses and more of the seed/static-literal shells in the production lowering path. `todo_mvc` no longer hand-builds its main-input/edit-focus/edit-title/focus-hint mirror nodes or several of its repeated empty/bool/tag/seed literals, and the counter accumulator runtime no longer hand-builds its initial seed literal or mirror-sink bridge cells; they now route through shared `append_literal(...)` and `append_mirror_cell(...)`, and `rg` now shows `IrNodeKind::MirrorCell` only inside that shared helper.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining raw `Literal` construction beneath the shared helper layer. The shared append-list runtime, `circle_drawer`, the direct `temperature_converter` / `flight_booker` / `timer` lowerers, and the timed-counter accumulator helpers no longer hand-build their local `IrNodeKind::Literal(...)` nodes; they now route those through shared `append_literal(...)`, and `rg` now shows `IrNodeKind::Literal(...)` only inside that helper itself.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the direct form-runtime family’s remaining wrapper shell through one shared builder-driven lowering entry. `temperature_converter`, `flight_booker`, and `timer` no longer each carry their own bespoke “build IR then feed `lower_form_runtime_variant_program(...)`” wrapper; they now route through shared `lower_form_runtime_variant_from_builder(...)`, leaving those per-surface entries as builder-plus-converter selections rather than repeated lowering shells.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the form-runtime family’s public typed entrypoints through the same shared config-owned lowering path. `try_lower_temperature_converter(...)`, `try_lower_flight_booker(...)`, and `try_lower_timer(...)` no longer bounce through per-surface `*_program_from_expressions(...)` wrappers; they now route through shared `lower_form_runtime_variant_typed_program(...)` plus the existing `FormRuntimeVariantAttemptConfig` family configs.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the toggle-selected-list semantic family’s remaining duplicated runtime/program tail. `lower_toggle_selected_list_semantic_ir(...)` no longer assembles the bool-toggle runtime config, program config, and `lower_toggle_selected_list_program(...)` call separately in each semantic branch; the branch-specific logic now only derives persistence plus true/false values, and one shared semantic-family tail owns the runtime/program lowering path for both `StaticStrings` and retained-filter modes.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the counter semantic family’s remaining duplicated accumulator-program tail. `lower_counter(...)` no longer constructs `lower_single_action_counter_accumulator_program(...)` separately inside the `LATEST |> Math/sum()` and `HOLD` branches; the branch-specific logic now only derives initial value, increment delta, and persistence mode, and one shared semantic-family tail owns the accumulator-program lowering path for both counter shapes.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the interval timer-backed signal family through one shared family-owned lowering path. The production pipeline no longer probes separate `lower_interval_contextual_attempt` and `lower_interval_hold_contextual_attempt` wrappers; `lower_interval_family_step(...)` now iterates shared `INTERVAL_SIGNAL_FAMILY_CONFIGS` through `lower_interval_signal_variant_program(...)` / `lower_interval_signal_lowered_program(...)`, while the public `try_lower_interval(...)` and `try_lower_interval_hold(...)` entrypoints also route through that same shared family helper instead of their own contextual wrappers.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the interval family’s public typed entrypoints through that same shared config-owned path. `try_lower_interval(...)` and `try_lower_interval_hold(...)` no longer call `lower_interval_signal_variant_program(...)` directly; they now route through shared `lower_interval_signal_typed_program(...)` plus the existing `INTERVAL_SIGNAL_CONFIG` / `INTERVAL_HOLD_SIGNAL_CONFIG` family configs.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the timed-flow family through one shared family-owned lowering path. The production pipeline no longer probes separate `then` / `when` / `while` contextual wrappers even though all three already shared `lower_timed_flow_variant_program(...)`; `lower_timed_flow_family_step(...)` now iterates shared `TIMED_FLOW_VARIANT_FAMILY_CONFIGS` through `lower_timed_flow_variant_lowered_program(...)`, while the public `try_lower_then(...)`, `try_lower_when(...)`, and `try_lower_while(...)` entrypoints now route straight to their shared typed lowering helpers instead of bouncing back through contextual attempt wrappers.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the timed-flow family’s public typed entrypoints through that same shared config-owned path. `try_lower_then(...)`, `try_lower_when(...)`, and `try_lower_while(...)` no longer bounce through per-surface `lower_*_program_from_expressions(...)` wrappers; they now route through shared `lower_timed_flow_variant_typed_program(...)` plus the existing `TimedFlowVariantAttemptConfig` family configs.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the generic-host portion of the display family through one shared family-owned lowering path. The production display step no longer probes separate contextual wrappers for `pages` and `latest`; `lower_display_family_step(...)` now iterates shared `DISPLAY_GENERIC_HOST_FAMILY_CONFIGS` through `lower_generic_host_surface_family_program(...)`, while the remaining display shapes fall through to the smaller fallback attempt list. That moves another shipped production-path pair off per-surface family probing and into shared lowerer-owned config-plus-wrapper handling.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the single-sink-value portion of the display family through one shared family-owned lowering path. The production display step no longer probes separate contextual wrappers for `fibonacci` and `static`; it now iterates shared `DISPLAY_SINGLE_SINK_FAMILY_CONFIGS` through `lower_bindings_single_sink_value_family_program(...)`, which reuses shared `BindingsSingleSinkValueFamilyConfig` plus named sink-derivation/wrap functions instead of routing those two shipped cases through separate per-surface family attempts.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the sink-value-backed display production path itself instead of keeping `layers` as a one-off branch inside the display step. The production display step no longer calls a dedicated `lower_layers_display_family_program(...)`; it now iterates shared `DISPLAY_SINK_VALUES_FAMILY_CONFIGS` through `lower_generic_host_surface_with_sink_values_family_program(...)`, while `try_lower_layers(...)` continues to use that same shared sink-values family path through the shared config builder.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the display family’s remaining fallback surfaces through shared family-owned config layers. The production display step no longer carries a fallback attempt list for `cells` and `circle_drawer`; it now iterates shared direct-lowered `DISPLAY_DIRECT_FAMILY_CONFIGS` for `cells` and shared generic-host-IR `DISPLAY_GENERIC_HOST_IR_FAMILY_CONFIGS` for `circle_drawer`, while `try_lower_circle_drawer(...)` also routes through shared `GenericHostIrFamilyConfig` typing instead of bouncing through a contextual wrapper.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the append-list subgroup through shared lowerer-owned family helpers instead of per-surface contextual attempts. The production list step no longer probes separate `lower_list_retain_count_contextual_attempt`, `lower_list_retain_remove_contextual_attempt`, or `lower_shopping_list_contextual_attempt` wrappers; it now routes those shipped surfaces through shared `lower_append_list_family_program(...)` plus dedicated subgroup family helpers, and the public `try_lower_list_retain_count(...)`, `try_lower_list_retain_remove(...)`, and `try_lower_shopping_list(...)` entrypoints now route through the same family-owned lowering path instead of bouncing through contextual attempt wrappers.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the append-list subgroup’s remaining dedicated wrapper layer through shared family configs. The production list step no longer treats `list_retain_count`, `list_retain_remove`, and `shopping_list` as three special-case append-list attempts; it now iterates shared `LIST_APPEND_LIST_FAMILY_CONFIGS` through `lower_append_list_surface_family_program(...)`, and the public typed entrypoints for those three shipped surfaces now route through those same shared append-list family configs instead of carrying dedicated wrapper functions.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the append-list subgroup’s public typed path through the same shared config-owned entry. `try_lower_list_retain_count(...)`, `try_lower_list_retain_remove(...)`, and `try_lower_shopping_list(...)` no longer each carry their own closure shell around `lower_append_list_surface_family_program(...)`; they now all route through shared `lower_append_list_surface_typed_program(...)` plus the existing append-list family configs.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the flat-stripe-backed list subgroup through shared lowerer-owned family configs instead of per-surface fallback attempts. The production list step no longer probes separate contextual wrappers for `list_map_external_dep`, `list_map_block`, `list_object_state`, or `list_retain_reactive`; it now iterates shared `LIST_BINDINGS_FLAT_STRIPE_FAMILY_CONFIGS` and `LIST_FLAT_STRIPE_HOST_ONLY_FAMILY_CONFIGS`, and the public `try_lower_list_map_external_dep(...)`, `try_lower_list_map_block(...)`, `try_lower_list_object_state(...)`, and `try_lower_list_retain_reactive(...)` entrypoints now route through those same shared flat-stripe family helpers instead of bouncing through per-surface contextual attempts.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining list-family fallback shapes through shared family configs instead of a raw fallback-attempt tail. The production list step no longer keeps per-surface fallback attempts for `todo_mvc`, `chained_list_remove_bug`, or `crud`; it now iterates shared checkbox-list, template-backed-derived-sink, and titled-column family config arrays, and the public `try_lower_todo_mvc(...)` / `try_lower_crud(...)` entrypoints now route through shared typed family helpers instead of bouncing through contextual wrappers.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining path-backed semantic persistence derivation through shared config-owned collectors instead of ad hoc per-surface path stitching. `list_retain_reactive` and `todo_mvc` now both route their durable metadata through shared `collect_path_lowering_persistence_from_config(...)` / `collect_path_lowering_persistence_from_configs(...)` helpers plus lowerer-owned `LoweringPathPersistenceConfig` arrays, and the crate now includes focused shared coverage for collecting multiple durable hold/list-store configs from one semantic-family-owned config slice.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the counter family’s durable hold metadata through a shared binding-config collector instead of a one-off closure. `counter HOLD` lowering no longer hand-builds durable metadata through `collect_single_hold_binding_lowering_persistence(...)`; it now routes through shared `LoweringBindingPersistenceConfig` plus `collect_binding_lowering_persistence_from_config(...)`, keeping the counter semantic family on the same config-owned persistence path as the newer path-backed semantic families.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/cells_preview.rs` now also centralizes the `cells` durable override metadata through the same shared path-config persistence collector used by the lowerer-owned semantic families. The `cells` lowerer no longer calls `persist_entries_for_path(...)` directly for the overrides list-store metadata; it now routes through shared `LoweringPathPersistenceConfig` plus `collect_path_lowering_persistence_from_config(...)`, removing another per-surface persistence seam even though the direct `cells` lowering branch itself still remains.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the `cells` display branch through a lowerer-owned bindings family path instead of the old direct-family hook. The production display step no longer carries `DISPLAY_DIRECT_FAMILY_CONFIGS` / `lower_direct_family_program(...)` for `cells`; it now routes that shipped branch through shared `BindingsOnlyFamilyConfig` plus `lower_bindings_only_family_program(...)`, while `cells_preview::try_lower_cells_program_from_expressions(...)` also delegates through the same shared typed family helper instead of remaining its own top-level production-path lowerer.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also owns the shipped `cells` binding-builder semantics directly instead of leaving a duplicate production copy behind in `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/cells_preview.rs`. The `cells` production path still uses cells-specific source extraction, but those builder/extraction helpers now live only in `lower.rs` and `cells_preview.rs` is back to being a thin preview/runtime wrapper around `lower_cells_display_typed_program(...)` plus interactive preview behavior.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the timed `then` / `when` family’s durable input-hold metadata through a shared lowerer-owned persistence-seed shape instead of raw binding-path/slot arguments in the IR builder. `TimedFlowProgramConfig` now carries `input_a_persistence` / `input_b_persistence` as shared `LoweringPathPersistenceSeed` values, the hold-backed timed math runtime routes those seeds through shared `collect_path_lowering_persistence_from_seed(...)`, and the focused persistence-helper coverage now exercises that same seed path instead of the old `collect_single_hold_path_lowering_persistence(...)` one-off.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the shipped `cells` override durability config through the same shared persistence-config slice shape used by the newer semantic families. `build_cells_program_from_bindings(...)` no longer inlines its own `LoweringPathPersistenceConfig` value; it now routes `CellsProgram::OVERRIDES_LIST_HOLD_NODE` through shared `CELLS_PERSISTENCE_CONFIGS` plus `collect_path_lowering_persistence_from_configs(...)`, keeping the `cells` durable list-store path on the same config-owned collection path as `todo_mvc`, `list_retain_reactive`, and the timed-flow families.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining validation-only typed lowering shell behind a shared generic helper instead of leaving `todo_mvc_physical` on its own bespoke path. `try_lower_todo_mvc_physical_from_expressions(...)` no longer calls `lower_validation_only_surface(...)` with an inline `StructuralValidationSpec`; it now routes through shared `ValidationOnlyTypedConfig` plus `lower_validation_only_typed_program(...)`, moving that outlier off its one-off lowering wrapper and onto the same config-owned typed-entry shape as the other extracted families.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the toggle-selected semantic family’s durability ownership at the outer family-config layer instead of hiding it inside one semantic mode branch. `list_retain_reactive` no longer carries `LoweringPathPersistenceConfig` slices inside `ToggleSelectedListSemanticMode::RetainedIntegerFilter`; `ToggleSelectedListSemanticConfig` now owns persistence alongside the shared program config, so both `list_retain_reactive` and `list_map_external_dep` route persistence through the same family-owned `collect_path_lowering_persistence_from_configs(...)` call even though only the retained-filter variant currently persists.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the plain `counter` family’s durable hold metadata behind the same seed-style persistence ownership pattern used by the newer semantic helpers. The counter HOLD semantic branch no longer constructs an inline `LoweringBindingPersistenceConfig`; `CounterSemanticConfig` now owns a shared `LoweringBindingPersistenceSeed`, `lower_counter(...)` only returns the matched hold binding, and the real durable entry is derived once through shared `collect_binding_lowering_persistence_from_seed(...)` when the accumulator hold node exists.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the plain `counter` family’s semantic-shape dispatch behind config-owned extractor entries instead of keeping the `LATEST { ... } |> Math/sum()` vs `HOLD` match inside `lower_counter(...)`. `CounterSemanticConfig` now owns shared `CounterSemanticShapeConfig` entries for the two supported shapes, `lower_counter(...)` only orchestrates shared semantic extraction plus accumulator lowering, and the branch-specific parsing now lives in reusable shape helpers instead of the production lowering tail.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the shipped `cells` bindings-only branch through a shared bindings-plus-semantic-config family helper instead of leaving `build_cells_program_from_bindings(...)` as the direct production target of the family config. The production display step now routes `cells` through shared `BindingsWithSemanticConfigFamilyConfig`, the cells-specific required functions/bindings/title policy/durable overrides metadata now live in lowerer-owned `CellsLoweringConfig`, and the remaining source extraction runs through `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` rather than a raw standalone builder hook.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the plain `counter` branch’s generic-host family hook through the same config-owned pattern instead of leaving `build_counter_lowered_program(...)` as a raw production callback. The counter family now routes through shared `BindingsWithGenericHostIrSemanticConfigFamilyConfig`, `COUNTER_BINDINGS_GENERIC_HOST_IR_CONFIG` owns both the semantic config and the generic-host shell, and the old pre-semantic helper layer was removed once `lower_counter_program_from_config(...)` became the family-owned callback.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining `cells` semantic extraction behind a config-selected derive step instead of keeping title/header/default-formula derivation inline in the final builder. `CellsLoweringConfig` now owns `derive_cells_program_semantics(...)`, `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` is down to shared assembly plus persistence collection, and the cells production path no longer interprets source structure directly at the final family callback site.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the plain `counter` branch’s host-view construction behind a shared derived-source generic-host helper instead of leaving `build_counter_host_view(...)` as a per-surface builder. `COUNTER_HOST_VIEW_CONFIG` now owns the counter validation/sink/view-site metadata, `COUNTER_BINDINGS_GENERIC_HOST_IR_CONFIG` points at shared `lower_single_derived_source_generic_host_ir(...)`, and the counter family’s semantic config plus generic-host config now both live at the family-config layer.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells-specific validation/function-name policy at the config layer instead of hardcoding `cells`/`column_header`/`default_formula` diagnostics inside the extractor helpers. `CellsLoweringConfig` now owns the subset label plus semantic function names, and the cells extraction helpers route those values through the existing config-owned derive path so the production cells family no longer bakes those policy strings into helper bodies.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells field-derivation hooks at the config layer instead of letting `derive_cells_program_semantics(...)` know how to extract document title, headers, and default formulas itself. `CellsLoweringConfig` now owns shared derive callbacks for display title, column headers, and default formulas, and the cells extractor helpers reuse one shared top-level-function-body lookup path instead of inlining per-field function scans inside the production semantic tail.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells indexed-expression policy at the config layer instead of letting the evaluator hardcode `row` / `column_index`, `Text/empty`, and the `default_formula subset` diagnostics. `CellsLoweringConfig` now owns shared `IndexedStaticExpressionConfig`, `extract_cells_column_headers(...)` and `eval_cells_default_formula(...)` both route through one shared indexed-expression evaluator, and the helper layer no longer bakes those cells-specific alias/path/error strings into its control flow.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells document-title call-chain policy at the config layer instead of keeping a cells-only `Document/new(root: Element/stripe(items: ...))` walker inline. `CellsLoweringConfig` now owns shared `DocumentTitleTextConfig`, the production title derive step routes through reusable call-argument/list-item/text-argument helpers, and the helper layer no longer hardcodes the cells title path shape inside a bespoke source parser.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells grid-shape policy at the config layer instead of letting the semantic tail hardcode `row_count`, `col_count`, and the static-vs-dynamic title switch inline. `CellsLoweringConfig` now owns shared `CellsGridShapeConfig`, `derive_cells_program_semantics(...)` routes through `derive_cells_grid_shape(...)`, and the helper layer no longer bakes those cells-specific binding names/defaults/title-mode rules directly into the production semantic body.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells top-level document-call requirement at the config layer instead of keeping a bespoke `document: Document/new(...)` check in the semantic tail. `CellsLoweringConfig` now owns shared `BindingFunctionCallSpec`, `derive_cells_program_semantics(...)` routes through reusable `require_binding_function_call(...)`, and the title derive step reuses that same binding spec instead of hardcoding `document`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells top-level function-body lookup policy at the config layer instead of threading raw `column_header` / `default_formula` strings through extractor bodies. `CellsLoweringConfig` now owns shared `TopLevelFunctionBodySpec` entries for both fields, `extract_cells_column_headers(...)` and `extract_default_formulas(...)` route through reusable `require_top_level_function_body_spec(...)`, and the cells helper layer no longer bakes those top-level function names into its control flow or diagnostics.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells title-leaf text policy at the config layer instead of keeping a hardcoded `Element/label(label: ...)` lookup in the document-title extractor. `DocumentTitleTextConfig` now owns the leaf `FunctionCallArgumentStep`, `extract_document_title_text(...)` routes through that shared config-owned text-argument spec, and the cells helper layer no longer bakes the final label path/argument names into its control flow.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells dynamic-title trigger policy at the config layer instead of letting `derive_cells_grid_shape(...)` hardcode `row_count || col_count` to switch between `Cells` and `Cells Dynamic`. `CellsGridShapeConfig` now owns shared `dynamic_title_bindings`, and the grid-shape helper no longer bakes those title-trigger bindings into its control flow.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells indexed-text coercion policy behind one shared helper instead of letting both header extraction and default-formula extraction each match on `Text` / `Number` / `Bool`. `extract_cells_column_headers(...)` and `extract_default_formulas(...)` now both route through shared `eval_indexed_static_expression_as_text(...)`, and the cells helper layer no longer duplicates that text-coercion control flow or its error formatting.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells literal binding/default policy behind one shared config-owned binding spec instead of letting `derive_cells_grid_shape(...)` thread separate `row_count_binding`, `default_row_count`, `col_count_binding`, and `default_col_count` fields through helper calls. `CellsGridShapeConfig` now owns shared `LiteralU32BindingSpec` entries, and the grid-shape helper now routes both dimensions through reusable `binding_u32_literal_or_default_spec(...)`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells title-path extraction wrapper behind one shared nested list-item text helper instead of keeping a dedicated `extract_document_title_text(...)` shell for the production display-title step. `derive_cells_display_title(...)` now routes directly through reusable `nested_list_item_text_argument(...)` plus config-owned `FunctionCallArgumentStep` slices, and the cells helper layer no longer needs a dedicated title wrapper function.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells binding-driven title lookup behind one shared helper instead of letting `derive_cells_display_title(...)` reach directly into the binding map and `DocumentTitleTextConfig` fields. The production display-title step now routes through reusable `binding_nested_list_item_text_argument(...)`, so the cells semantic path no longer owns that binding lookup/plumbing inline.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells text-argument stepping behind shared `FunctionCallArgumentStep` helpers instead of letting `nested_list_item_text_argument(...)` unpack raw `path` and `argument_name` fields itself. The production title path now routes through reusable `function_call_argument_step(...)` and `function_call_text_argument(...)`, so that cells extraction seam no longer deconstructs those config-owned step specs inline.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells title-text extraction policy behind a config-owned callback instead of hardcoding `first_text_literal(...)` inside the shared function-call helper. `DocumentTitleTextConfig` now owns the text extractor, `binding_nested_list_item_text_argument(...)` routes that callback through reusable `function_call_text_argument(...)`, and the production display-title path no longer bakes its literal-text selection rule into the helper body.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells text-argument extraction spec behind one config-owned value instead of threading a raw `FunctionCallArgumentStep` and a separate callback through the shared helper signature. `DocumentTitleTextConfig` now owns a shared `FunctionCallTextArgumentConfig`, and `binding_nested_list_item_text_argument(...)` now routes through `function_call_text_argument(...)` with that single spec rather than passing step/extractor plumbing separately.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells nested-list locator spec behind one config-owned value instead of threading raw `argument_steps` plus `list_item_index` through the title helper. `DocumentTitleTextConfig` now owns a shared `NestedListItemArgumentConfig`, and `binding_nested_list_item_text_argument(...)` now routes through `nested_list_item_argument(...)` with that single locator spec rather than passing the step slice and item index separately.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells binding-plus-list-item title source behind one config-owned value instead of keeping the binding spec and nested-list locator as separate fields on `DocumentTitleTextConfig`. The production title path now routes through shared `BindingNestedListItemArgumentConfig`, and both `derive_cells_program_semantics(...)` and `binding_nested_list_item_text_argument(...)` now read the same source spec instead of unpacking `binding` and `list_item` independently.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells binding-plus-list-item lookup behind one shared helper instead of letting `binding_nested_list_item_text_argument(...)` reach directly into the binding map and nested-list source config. The production title path now routes through reusable `binding_nested_list_item_argument(...)`, so that cells extraction seam no longer owns the binding lookup plus nested-list locator plumbing inline.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells top-level indexed text-field evaluation behind one shared helper instead of letting both `extract_cells_column_headers(...)` and `extract_default_formulas(...)` each pass the same subset/expression/function-name wiring into `eval_indexed_static_expression_as_text(...)`. Both production extractors now route through reusable `eval_top_level_indexed_text_field(...)`, so that cells extraction seam no longer duplicates the same top-level indexed text evaluation call shape inline.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells title-source validation path behind one shared helper instead of letting `derive_cells_program_semantics(...)` peel the binding requirement out of `config.document_title.source.binding` directly. The production semantic tail now routes through reusable `require_binding_nested_list_item_source(...)`, so the shared title source config is consumed consistently in both validation and lookup paths.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells top-level indexed text-field specs behind one grouped config instead of carrying `column_headers` and `default_formulas` as separate sibling fields on `CellsLoweringConfig`. The production extractors now read both specs through shared `CellsIndexedTextFieldsConfig`, so that cells field-spec plumbing no longer stays split across separate top-level config slots.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining cells semantic sub-configs behind one grouped config instead of carrying `document_title`, `grid_shape`, and `indexed_text_fields` as separate sibling fields on `CellsLoweringConfig`. The production semantic tail and its helpers now read those knobs through shared `CellsSemanticConfig`, so the remaining cells semantics are less split across parallel top-level config fields.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the `list_retain_count` append-list IR specialization behind the shared append-list runtime config instead of keeping that shipped surface on a bespoke `build_list_retain_count_ir(...)` production callback. The append-list runtime now owns derived count sinks through shared `AppendListDerivedCountConfig` / `AppendListDerivedListSpec`, and `list_retain_count` now routes through `lower_append_list_ephemeral_program(...)` like the other append-list family members.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the append-list family’s production IR entry itself instead of keeping a per-surface `build_ir` callback slot on `AppendListFamilyConfig`. With `list_retain_count`, `list_retain_remove`, and `shopping_list` all now using the same shared append-list runtime path, the family helper itself now always materializes IR through `lower_append_list_ephemeral_program(...)`, so append-list production lowering no longer advertises per-surface IR construction hooks.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the `cells` family’s semantic entry itself instead of keeping per-surface semantic callback slots on `CellsLoweringConfig`. The shipped `cells` path no longer carries `derive_grid_shape`, `derive_display_title`, `derive_column_headers`, `derive_default_formulas`, or `derive_semantics` callback hooks through config; it now routes straight through the shared `derive_cells_*` helpers, so that family no longer advertises per-surface semantic assembly callbacks in the production path.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the remaining `cells` top-level indexed-text traversal behind one shared collector instead of letting `extract_default_formulas(...)` and `extract_cells_column_headers(...)` each repeat the same top-level function-body lookup and row/column walk shape. Both production helpers now route through shared `collect_top_level_indexed_text_grid(...)`, so that cells field traversal seam no longer stays duplicated across the two shipped indexed-text extractors.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the `cells` grid-shape derivation behind one shared lowerer-owned helper instead of keeping `derive_cells_grid_shape(...)` as a dedicated per-surface production function. The shipped `cells` config now uses shared `LiteralU32GridShapeConfig` plus `BindingPresenceTitleConfig`, and the semantic tail derives title/row/column shape through reusable `derive_literal_u32_grid_shape(...)`, so that grid-shape seam no longer stays cells-only logic in the production path.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the `cells` display-title fallback path behind one shared lowerer-owned helper instead of keeping `derive_cells_display_title(...)` as a dedicated per-surface production function. The semantic tail now routes straight through reusable `binding_nested_list_item_text_argument_or_default(...)`, so that title fallback seam no longer stays as a cells-only wrapper around the shared nested-list text extraction path.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the `cells` nested-list title text config itself behind a lowerer-owned generic name instead of keeping that path framed as a document-title-specific surface helper. The shipped `cells` title path now uses shared `NestedListItemTextConfig`, and the semantic tail plus fallback helper now route through generic `binding_nested_list_item_text(...)` / `binding_nested_list_item_text_or_default(...)`, so that remaining text extraction seam is less tied to the `cells` document-title surface naming.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the toggle-selected list semantic family’s production mode dispatch behind one lowerer-owned semantic enum instead of keeping per-surface `derive_values` callbacks and parallel optional payload slots on `ToggleSelectedListSemanticConfig`. `list_map_external_dep` and `list_retain_reactive` now choose shared `ToggleSelectedListSemanticMode::StaticValues(...)` / `RetainedIntegerFilter(...)`, and `lower_toggle_selected_list_semantic_ir(...)` performs the family-owned match itself before building the shared toggle runtime and persistence path.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the plain `counter` family’s production semantic-shape dispatch behind one lowerer-owned shape enum instead of keeping config-owned `derive` callbacks on `CounterSemanticShapeConfig`. `CounterSemanticConfig` now carries shared `CounterSemanticShape::LatestSum` / `Hold` entries, and `derive_counter_semantics(...)` performs the family-owned match itself before building the shared accumulator runtime and hold-persistence path.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the single-sink display family’s production sink-value dispatch behind one lowerer-owned mode enum instead of keeping per-surface `derive_sink_value` callbacks on `BindingsSingleSinkValueFamilyConfig`. `fibonacci` and `static` now choose shared `BindingsSingleSinkValueMode::FibonacciMessage` / `StaticDocument`, and `derive_bindings_single_sink_value(...)` performs the family-owned match itself before the shared single-sink host-view lowering path materializes the retained document.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the template-backed derived host-view family’s production sink/template dispatch behind one lowerer-owned mode enum instead of keeping `todo_mvc` on function-pointer fields inside `TemplateBackedDerivedSinkHostViewConfig`.
