The shared config now chooses `TemplateBackedDerivedSinkHostViewMode::TodoMvc`, and the family-owned match now performs the sink derivation plus template materialization before the shared template-backed retained host-view path runs.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the flat-stripe semantic-IR list family’s production IR dispatch behind the family helper itself instead of keeping a `lower_ir` callback on `SemanticIrFlatStripeFamilyConfig`. `list_map_external_dep` and `list_retain_reactive` already shared `ToggleSelectedListSemanticConfig` plus `lower_toggle_selected_list_semantic_ir(...)`; the config no longer needs to carry that function pointer, and the family-owned lowering path now performs the shared toggle semantic IR build directly before wrapping the retained flat-stripe host view.

- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the path-backed persistent-IR semantic wrapper itself instead of keeping `todo_mvc` on a bespoke one-off helper. `todo_mvc` no longer routes through `TodoUiStateSemanticConfig` plus `lower_todo_ui_state_semantic_ir(...)`; it now uses shared `PersistentIrPathConfig` plus `lower_persistent_ir_from_path_configs(...)`, which collects lowerer-owned path persistence and feeds it into a fixed IR builder. That removes another per-surface semantic wrapper from the production lowering spine while preserving the same durable `store.todos` metadata.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the toggle-selected semantic family’s mode dispatch at the config layer instead of carrying a mixed semantic-shape enum through the production lowerer. `list_map_external_dep` and `list_retain_reactive` still share `lower_toggle_selected_list_semantic_ir(...)`, but the shipped configs now choose specialized derive helpers directly, so the production path no longer matches on `StaticStrings` vs `RetainedIntegerFilter` before lowering the shared toggle runtime and persistence path.

- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the shipped `cells` persistence path through the shared persistent-IR helper instead of having `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` collect path persistence inline and hand-assemble an empty IR shell. `CellsLoweringConfig` now carries a shared `PersistentIrPathConfig`, `cells` routes through `lower_persistent_ir_from_path_configs(...)` like `todo_mvc`, and empty retained IR shells now come from one reusable `build_empty_persistent_ir_program(...)` helper.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the shipped `cells` indexed-text traversal shape behind shared lowerer-owned grid config instead of letting the column-header and default-formula extractors hardcode separate row-range wiring. `CellsIndexedTextFieldsConfig` now carries shared `TopLevelIndexedTextGridConfig` entries with `IndexedTextGridRowRange`, and `derive_cells_program_semantics(...)` now routes both shipped indexed-text fields through one reusable `derive_cells_indexed_text_fields(...)` / `collect_top_level_indexed_text_grid_from_config(...)` path.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the shipped `cells` title-plus-grid-frame derivation behind one shared lowerer-owned helper instead of assembling title, display title, row count, and column count ad hoc inside `derive_cells_program_semantics(...)`. The `cells` semantic path now routes through reusable `derive_titled_literal_u32_grid_semantics(...)`, which composes the shared `LiteralU32GridShapeConfig` and `NestedListItemTextConfig` helpers before the remaining field-specific lowering runs.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the last extra grid-shape wrapper from that shipped `cells` frame path. `derive_titled_literal_u32_grid_semantics(...)` now reads row count, column count, and title directly from the shared `LiteralU32GridShapeConfig` pieces instead of bouncing through a separate `LiteralU32GridShape` struct plus `derive_literal_u32_grid_shape(...)`, so one more production-only semantic layer is gone from the `cells` lowering spine.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the shipped `cells` default-formula baseline-state derivation behind the indexed-text helper instead of rebuilding `CellsFormulaState` inline in `derive_cells_program_semantics(...)`. `derive_cells_indexed_text_fields(...)` now owns both parsed `default_formulas` and the derived baseline state, so the remaining top-level `cells` semantic tail consumes one shared indexed-text lowering result instead of reassembling persistence-adjacent formula state itself.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also collapses the shipped `cells` nested-list title extraction stack behind one shared helper instead of bouncing through separate `binding_nested_list_item_text(...)`, `binding_nested_list_item_text_or_default(...)`, and `require_nested_list_item_text_or_default(...)` wrappers. The `cells` frame path now routes directly through reusable `require_binding_nested_list_item_text_or_default(...)`, which validates the shared binding source and applies the shared text-argument/default logic in one place.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also centralizes the shipped `cells` indexed-text evaluation plumbing behind the shared static-expression text evaluator instead of letting the shared grid collector depend on the full `CellsLoweringConfig`. `derive_cells_indexed_text_fields(...)` now passes only the validation subset and `IndexedStaticExpressionConfig`, while `collect_top_level_indexed_text_grid_from_config(...)` / `collect_indexed_text_grid(...)` now operate on those shared lowerer-owned inputs directly.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the extra `derive_cells_program_semantics(...)` aggregation layer from the shipped `cells` entry point. `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` now composes structural validation, `derive_titled_literal_u32_grid_semantics(...)`, `derive_cells_indexed_text_fields(...)`, and the shared persistent-IR helper directly instead of bouncing through another production-only semantic wrapper.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining `cells` frame/result wrapper structs from the shipped entry point. `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` now reads row count, column count, title, and display title directly from the shared grid-shape and nested-list helpers, and `derive_cells_indexed_text_fields(...)` now returns the indexed-text triple directly instead of wrapping those values in `TitledLiteralU32GridSemantics` and `CellsIndexedTextFieldLowering`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the nested top-level function-body wrapper from the shipped `cells` indexed-text config. `TopLevelIndexedTextGridConfig` now carries the function name directly, the shared grid collector calls `require_top_level_function_body(...)` directly, and the shipped `cells` config no longer bounces through `TopLevelFunctionBodySpec` just to recover the same string.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining config-unpacking shim from the shipped `cells` indexed-text path. `derive_cells_indexed_text_fields(...)` now passes the function name and row-range directly into shared `collect_top_level_indexed_text_grid(...)`, so the production path no longer needs a `collect_top_level_indexed_text_grid_from_config(...)` wrapper just to peel `TopLevelIndexedTextGridConfig` back apart.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining `derive_cells_indexed_text_fields(...)` aggregation layer from the shipped `cells` entry point. `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` now composes the shared indexed-text collector and baseline-state derivation directly instead of bouncing through another cells-only helper that only reassembled `column_headers`, parsed `default_formulas`, and `CellsFormulaState`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining indexed-text row-bounds shim from the shared `cells` traversal path. `collect_top_level_indexed_text_grid(...)` now expands `IndexedTextGridRowRange` itself instead of bouncing through a separate `indexed_text_grid_row_bounds(...)` helper before entering the shared indexed-text evaluator.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also merges the remaining two-step indexed-text collector chain into one shared helper. The shipped `cells` entry point now calls `collect_indexed_text_grid(...)` directly, and that helper now owns top-level body lookup, row-range expansion, and grid traversal instead of bouncing through a `collect_top_level_indexed_text_grid(...)` wrapper first.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining text-coercion wrapper from the shared `cells` indexed evaluator path. `collect_indexed_text_grid(...)` now handles `IndexedStaticValue::{Text, Number, Bool}` directly after `eval_indexed_static_expression(...)`, so the production path no longer bounces through `eval_indexed_static_expression_as_text(...)`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining `CellsSemanticConfig` wrapper from the shipped `cells` lowering path. `CellsLoweringConfig` now carries the shared document-title, grid-shape, and indexed-text configs directly, and `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` reads those shared lowerer-owned knobs without bouncing through another cells-only semantic container.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining cells-only default-formula accumulation loop from the shipped `cells` entry point. `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` now routes parsed default-formula collection through shared `collect_non_empty_parsed_indexed_text_grid(...)` instead of hand-rolling another per-surface `collect_indexed_text_grid(...)` plus `if !text.is_empty()` loop before baseline-state derivation.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also merges the remaining text-grid collector split into one shared mapped-grid helper. `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` now routes both column headers and parsed default formulas through `collect_mapped_indexed_text_grid(...)`, so the shipped `cells` path no longer depends on parallel text-only and parsed-text collector layers.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining inline `cells` frame-derivation bundle from the shipped entry point. `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` now routes row count, column count, title, and display title through shared `derive_titled_u32_grid_frame(...)` keyed by the lowerer-owned title/grid configs instead of assembling that semantic tuple inline at the production call site.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining inline `cells` formula-state assembly from the shipped entry point. `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` now routes parsed default-formula collection plus baseline-state derivation through shared `derive_cells_default_formulas_and_baseline_state(...)` instead of building `default_formulas` and `CellsFormulaState::from_lowered_formulas(...)` inline at the production call site.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining inline header-value extraction pass from the shipped `cells` entry point. `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` now routes the header path through shared `collect_mapped_indexed_text_values(...)` instead of collecting indexed `(row, column, text)` pairs and stripping coordinates inline with `map(|(_, header)| header)`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining inline formula-map collection pass from the shipped `cells` formula helper. `derive_cells_default_formulas_and_baseline_state(...)` now routes parsed formula collection through shared `collect_mapped_indexed_text_map(...)` instead of collecting indexed pairs and materializing the `BTreeMap` inline before baseline-state derivation.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining bespoke top-level binding lookup path from the shipped `counter` lowering family. The lowerer now has one shared `require_top_level_binding_expr(...)` helper, `require_binding_function_call(...)` reuses it, and `lower_counter_program_from_config(...)` no longer hand-assembles its own top-level `document` / `counter` lookup errors.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining bespoke top-level binding / function lookup paths from the shipped `fibonacci`, timed-flow, and `interval` families. The lowerer now has one shared `require_top_level_function_expr(...)` helper alongside `require_top_level_binding_expr(...)`, `derive_fibonacci_message_sink_value(...)` no longer hand-rolls its own top-level `fibonacci` / `position` / `result` / `message` / `document` lookups, `lower_timed_flow_family_base(...)` no longer reassembles `input_a` / `input_b` binding errors inline, and `lower_interval_signal_mode(...)` no longer hand-assembles `document` / `tick` / `counter` top-level errors.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining `CellsIndexedTextFieldsConfig` wrapper from the shipped `cells` lowering path. `CellsLoweringConfig` now carries the shared `TopLevelIndexedTextGridConfig` entries for `column_headers` and `default_formulas` directly, and `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` reads those lowerer-owned knobs without bouncing through another cells-only config layer.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining `LiteralU32GridShapeConfig` wrapper from the shipped `cells` lowering path. `CellsLoweringConfig` now carries the shared `LiteralU32BindingSpec` row/column knobs plus `BindingPresenceTitleConfig` directly, and `derive_titled_u32_grid_frame(...)` now reads those lowerer-owned specs without bouncing through another cells-only grid-shape container.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining bespoke root-document lookup path from generic HostView lowering. - `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining primitive title/grid config wrappers from the shipped `cells` lowering path. `CellsLoweringConfig` now carries the row/column binding names, defaults, and dynamic-title knobs directly, `derive_titled_u32_grid_frame(...)` now reads those lowerer-owned primitive specs directly, and the shared `binding_presence_title(...)` helper now works on the primitive title inputs instead of a cells-only wrapper struct.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining cells-only frame assembly helper from the shipped `cells` entry point. `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` now composes the shared row/column literal readers, shared dynamic-title helper, and shared nested-list text extractor directly instead of bouncing through `derive_titled_u32_grid_frame(...)`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining cells-only default-formula/baseline-state helper from the shipped `cells` entry point. `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` now composes the shared mapped indexed-text collector plus `CellsFormulaState::from_lowered_formulas(...)` directly instead of bouncing through `derive_cells_default_formulas_and_baseline_state(...)`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining inline formula-map collector wrapper from the shipped `cells` entry point. `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` now routes parsed default formulas through the shared `collect_mapped_indexed_text_grid(...)` collector directly and materializes the `BTreeMap` at the call site instead of bouncing through `collect_mapped_indexed_text_map(...)`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining `TopLevelIndexedTextGridConfig` wrapper from the shipped `cells` lowering path. `CellsLoweringConfig` now carries the indexed-grid function names and row-range knobs directly, and `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` reads those lowerer-owned primitive inputs without bouncing through another cells-only config layer.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining document-title wrapper stack from the shipped `cells` lowering path. `CellsLoweringConfig` now carries the document-title binding, argument-step slice, item index, and text-extractor primitives directly, and `require_binding_nested_list_item_text_or_default(...)` now routes through those lowerer-owned inputs without bouncing through `BindingNestedListItemArgumentConfig`, `NestedListItemArgumentConfig`, or `FunctionCallTextArgumentConfig`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining document-title binding-spec wrapper from the shipped `cells` lowering path. `CellsLoweringConfig` now carries the document-title binding name and binding path directly, and `require_binding_nested_list_item_text_or_default(...)` / `require_binding_function_call(...)` now route through those lowerer-owned primitive inputs without bouncing through `BindingFunctionCallSpec`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining document-title argument-step wrapper from the shipped `cells` lowering path. `CellsLoweringConfig` now carries the document-title argument paths, argument names, and text-argument path/name primitives directly, and the title extraction helpers now route through those lowerer-owned inputs without bouncing through `FunctionCallArgumentStep`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining cells-only document-title wrapper layer from the shipped `cells` entry point. `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` now validates the `document` binding through shared `require_binding_function_call(...)` and derives `display_title` directly from the shared nested-list/argument walkers instead of bouncing through `require_binding_nested_list_item_text_or_default(...)`.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining extra binding lookup from the shipped `cells` document-title path. `require_binding_function_call(...)` now returns the validated top-level binding expression, and `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` derives `display_title` from that shared validated expression instead of validating and then looking the same binding up again.
- `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs` now also removes the remaining nested-list title wrapper layer from the shipped `cells` document-title path. `lower_cells_program_from_config(...)` now derives `display_title` directly from the shared validated binding expression plus the shared function-call argument walker instead of bouncing through `nested_list_item_argument(...)` and `list_item_at_index(...)`.

- Removed the manual case-label layer from the shared family core in `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs`; `SurfaceProgramFamilyConfig<...>` and `BindingsProgramFamilyConfig<...>` now derive their subset key from generic config payloads through one shared `LoweringSubset` trait, case lookup no longer depends on a dedicated `label` field, and typed-entry mismatch reporting now reuses the generic subset carried by the selected lowering config instead of duplicating a second hard-coded matched-subset string beside the shared family data.
- Removed the direct raw-case-table selector calls from the shipped typed entrypoints in `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs`; the public example-specific typed lowerers now route through shared `SurfaceProgramGroup<...>` / `BindingsProgramGroup<...>` lookup helpers instead of calling `surface_program_case(...)` or `bindings_program_case(...)` against raw case arrays themselves, so typed selection now also flows through the shared group model rather than an example-specific case-array seam.

- Merged the remaining same-shape shipped surface inventories in `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs`; pages/latest plus the generic-toggle examples now route through one shared `GENERIC_HOST_SURFACE_CASES`, filter/checkbox/chained-checkbox now route through one shared `CHECKBOX_LIST_SURFACE_CASES`, and circle-drawer plus complex-counter now route through one shared `GENERIC_HOST_IR_SURFACE_CASES`, so production routing no longer carries separate same-shape display/toggle/counter case tables.

- Removed the last registry-shell layer from `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs`; `LoweringFamilyRegistry` and `lower_family_registry(...)` are gone, `LOWERING_PIPELINE` is now a direct ordered list of generic `&dyn LoweringFamilyGroup`, and the old single-purpose `*_REGISTRY` wrapper constants were deleted, so the production classifier now walks the generic group model directly instead of routing through one-off registry shells above the remaining case tables.
- Removed the remaining named bindings case-table layer from `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs`; the shipped `todo_mvc`, `cells`, and `counter` single-case bindings families plus the shipped `list_map_external_dep` / `list_retain_reactive` and `fibonacci` / `static` multi-case bindings families now inline their subset inventory directly inside their owning generic `BindingsProgramGroup<...>` literals instead of routing through separate `*_CASES` constants, so the remaining explicit production case-table inventory is now limited to surface/control-flow families.
- Removed the last standalone surface case-table constants from `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/lower.rs`; the shipped flat-stripe host-only, append-list, titled-column, display-sink-value, generic-host, checkbox-list, generic-host-IR, form-runtime, interval, and timed-flow families now all inline their subset inventory directly inside their owning generic `SurfaceProgramGroup<...>` literals, so `lower.rs` no longer carries any standalone `*_CASES` production inventory constants at all.

- Started Phase 2 in the live execution path: `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/ir_executor.rs` now drains dirty work through an ordered next-frontier scheduler instead of keeping an ever-broadening dirty set and broad-scanning the node list on each pass, and a new focused executor test proves that an unrelated branch is not revisited when a source pulse only touches the other dependency closure.
- Continued Phase 2 in the live execution path: `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/ir_executor.rs` now stores per-node values, link cells, math-accumulator inputs, list identities, and test-only evaluation counts in dense slot-backed vectors instead of node-id keyed `BTreeMap`s, routes dependency/source/mirror bookkeeping through slot indices, and drains an explicit ordered ready frontier round-by-round so same-batch sibling updates still reach deterministic quiescence. Focused executor tests now prove both that an unrelated branch is not revisited after a source pulse and that reversed dirty-root order reaches the same quiescent result, while the real `todo_mvc` append/edit preview flows stay green under the slot-backed scheduler.
- Continued Phase 2 again in the live execution path: `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/ir_executor.rs` now carries explicit cutoff state for source-pulse slots on top of the slot-backed ready frontier, rejecting stale source pulses whose `CausalSeq` is not newer than the accepted cutoff while preserving retained dependency-mirror rewrites. Focused executor tests now prove both stale source rejection across batches and stable one-batch quiescence when a stale source pulse is mixed into the batch, and the full crate suite remains green.
- Continued Phase 2 again in the live execution path: `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/ir_executor.rs` now drains accepted host inputs through explicit per-`CausalSeq` batch rounds instead of recomputing after every accepted message, so same-seq sibling inputs quiesce together while distinct pulse sequences still replay separately, and `LinkBind` now rejects stale rebinding attempts whose causal time is older than the live link state so a later-running stale bind cannot override a newer target. Focused executor tests now prove same-seq batch order reaches the same quiescent result while only recomputing the shared add node once, and stale link rebinds are ignored both across batches and when their slots run later, while the real batched counter flow and the full crate suite remain green.
- Continued Phase 2 again in the live execution path: `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/ir_executor.rs` now makes the live link-rebind cutoff rule explicit in one shared helper, and focused executor tests now prove the remaining same-seq dynamic-edge tie cases stay deterministic independent of host message order: `LATEST` keeps its declared input-order winner, and competing `LinkBind` updates keep the slot-order winner. The full crate suite remains green with those same-seq `LATEST` / `LINK` determinism proofs added.
- Continued Phase 2 again in the live execution path: `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/ir_executor.rs` now routes source-port, mirror-cell, and direct sink lookup through dense slot-backed tables instead of `BTreeMap` id lookups on the hot path, while keeping the existing bulk sink-value API stable for preview code. The new slot-backed dispatch path is green under focused batched-counter and same-seq-`LATEST` executor tests, `cargo check -p boon-engine-actors-lite`, and the full crate suite.
- Continued Phase 2 again in the live execution path: `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/ir_executor.rs` now routes `NodeId -> slot` through a dense slot-backed table too, so dependency wiring and `value(...)` / link-state lookup no longer depend on `BTreeMap<NodeId, NodeSlot>` in the hot path. The node-slot cut is green under focused dirty-closure, same-seq-`LATEST`, and real batched-counter executor tests, `cargo check -p boon-engine-actors-lite`, and the full crate suite.
- Continued Phase 2 again in the live execution path: `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/ir_executor.rs` now routes `FunctionId -> IrFunctionTemplate` lookup through a dense table instead of a `BTreeMap`, so direct `Call` / `ListMap` function-template resolution no longer depends on tree lookups in the executor hot path. The dense-function lookup cut is green under focused function-call and stable-list-map-instance tests, `cargo check -p boon-engine-actors-lite`, and the full crate suite.
- Continued Phase 2 again in the retained dependency path: `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/runtime.rs` now clamps recomputed retained member output sequences against the previously published state, so member replacement or dependency rewiring cannot regress `output_seq` when recompute runs from older preserved input/dependency sequences. Focused runtime tests now prove both the helper-level and full retained-runtime recompute paths preserve monotonic output sequences, and the full crate suite remains green.
- Continued Phase 2 again across the live/retained boundary: direct `MirrorWrite` slots in `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/ir_executor.rs` now honor the same cutoff discipline as source pulses, rejecting stale mirror writes on the generic executor hot path, while retained dependency snapshots in `crates/boon-engine-actors-lite/src/runtime.rs` explicitly reset mirror cutoffs before replaying a fresh dependency batch so older preserved dependency sequences can still drive the current retained value without regressing retained `output_seq`. Focused tests now prove both direct stale-mirror rejection and retained dependency replay across older preserved inputs, and the cells retained-runtime clear/restore plus structural-edit rebuild tests stay green under the split.
